Foreign Important Telegrams

India's Ruling Class Suppresses Resistance Movement

All Indian Congress Leaders Imprisoned

Bank Propaganda Funds Confiscated

Bombs Found on Darjeeling Express

Pinares Public Riot Leads to Bloodshed

Reuters, Bombay, 6th. The Indian government has completed the first step of a large-scale arrest of prominent leaders of the All-India Congress this morning, with approximately forty individuals apprehended, including nine women. Subsequently, the government declared the All-India Congress and its affiliated organizations in Bombay and Sindh illegal. While the situation here remains calm and businesses are closed, many merchants continue to place orders with British firms. New Delhi remains tranquil, although disturbances are anticipated within days, with Bombay expected to be the epicenter of the unrest. Sixteen individuals were detained in Kanpur today.

Reuters, Bombay, 6th. Sir Sykes, the Governor of Bombay Province, issued a public notice today, stating that the new law aims to curb the All-India Congress's interference with public freedoms and obstruction of government institutions. Law-abiding citizens need not fear, and the government is exerting every effort to suppress the All-India Congress's activities while striving to protect commerce from the impact of pickets and boycotts. According to reports from Karachi, foreign fabric merchants are deeply alarmed by the boycott news, leading to a significant decline in sales. One Indian merchant suffered a nervous breakdown due to intimidation. However, only four Indian-owned foreign fabric stores in Bombay were closed today, and public sentiment is gradually stabilizing. Authorities have begun severing the All-India Congress's funding sources. Two Indian-owned banks in Bombay, holding approximately 4,000 pounds of English gold deposited in private names by the All-India Congress, have been ordered by authorities not to allow withdrawals. The Governor of Bengal invited cloth merchants from Lahore to discuss methods for dissolving the picket line. The All-India Congress and its affiliated organizations in Madras have been dissolved by authorities, and gatherings are generally prohibited. This morning in Karachi, the dictator of the Congress led five volunteers to the seaside to disrupt salt laws without attracting public attention or police interference. The All-India Congress's only victory today was at a merchants' meeting in Calcutta, where extremist members, unwilling to defy European and Muslim opposition, passed a resolution to adjourn for two days, expressing opposition to the government's restoration and oppressive policies. Yesterday's riots in Pinales, due to police firing, resulted in two deaths and a hundred injuries. The county magistrate was struck by a stone thrown by the mob, and several police officers were also injured.

Reuters, Allahabad, 7th. Local authorities here have also adopted Bombay's methods, conducting a large-scale arrest of All-India Congress leaders. Starting at 3:30 AM this morning, a series of searches resulted in the detention of thirty individuals within an hour, including Gandhi's secretary Taishi and Gulangla's dictator Kosari. Immediately after Kosari's arrest, another dictator succeeded him, but he too will soon be imprisoned.

Reuters, Calcutta, 7th. Indian extremists have begun their activities today. This morning, when the Darjeeling Express arrived here, five bombs with detonating cords were found in a first-class compartment. According to reports from New Delhi, the ordinance declaring illegal societies has now been extended to the central provinces.

American Naval Hegemony Ambitions

Plans to Complete 100 New Ships Within Ten Years

Treaty-Permitted Tonnage, Transforming Pocket Battleships

Reuters, Washington, 4th. According to statements by Vinson, Chairman of the House Naval Committee, the American ten-year naval construction program will be submitted to the House today. This program stipulates that the United States will build 120 new ships within ten years at a cost of $616,250,000. All new ships, except for two aircraft carriers, will be used to replace ships that are old or obsolete. The program proposed by Vinson, already approved by the Naval Committee, also stipulates that $91.5 million be used to complete the construction of sixteen warships currently under construction, including seven 10,000-ton battleships with eight-inch guns.

Reuters, Washington, 6th. Secretary of the Navy Adams spoke before the House Naval Committee today, advocating the ten-year shipbuilding program, enabling the United States to achieve the strength permitted by the 1930 London Naval Treaty. According to reliable sources, the US government will instruct its representatives attending the Geneva Disarmament Conference on February 2nd to oppose any budgetary methods of disarmament, at least as far as the United States is concerned.

Reuters, Washington, 4th. According to Washington naval reporters, the US government has decided to build pocket battleships to replace cruisers. It is reported that orders have been issued to actively change the design of the 10,000-ton cruisers permitted by the treaty and currently under construction, so that they can be transformed into extremely small battleships, but with greater power than the recently completed Pensacola-class and Houston-class cruisers. An important naval officer stated today that once the new cruisers are modified, they will be stronger than any cruiser in the world, except for the German Deutschland.

European Reparations Conference

To Be Held in Lausanne on the 18th of This Month

Briand Unable to Attend Due to Illness

Reuters, London, 7th. It was learned today that after the British government proposed to various countries to hold a reparations conference in Lausanne, it has now received replies from various countries approving the proposal. January 18th was originally set as the formal opening date, but whether it will be possible to open the meeting on that day, or whether it will have to be delayed by one or two days, has not yet been determined, as France may want to postpone the meeting slightly. In addition to the United Kingdom, the participants in the reparations conference will be France, Italy, Belgium, Japan, Greece, Poland, Portugal, and Yugoslavia. Whether the United States will join has not yet been determined. Financial experts from Britain and France are now beginning talks, which are highly valued, as an understanding between these two countries can greatly assist the work of the conference.

Guomin, Paris, 7th. The rumors that French Foreign Minister Briand's illness is not minor have been indirectly confirmed today. Officials announced that Briand will not attend the Lausanne Conference and that Finance Minister Flandin will serve as the chief representative of France. French Premier Laval will only arrive at the opening and will immediately return to Paris. However, it is expected that Laval may visit Lausanne again at the time of the closing.

Political Instability in Spain

After Repeated Clashes Between Militia and Strikers, Disturbing Rumors Spread Throughout the Country, Saying That a Coup is About to Happen

Reuters, Madrid, 6th. After repeated clashes between the militia and strikers, frightening rumors have spread throughout the country, saying that a coup is about to happen. Today, many sources said that militia leader Sanjurjo is now planning to establish a dictatorship, and with the support of the military, he will seize supreme political power himself. Although Premier Azana denied that the militia had any plans to overthrow the government, public fear has not been diminished as a result. The public's antipathy towards the militia is now quite profound, especially in rural areas. Disturbances occurred in several places in Spain last night. In Arnedo, strikers clashed with the militia, resulting in the deaths of six men and women. Public anger is growing, and many believe that this turmoil is a sign that there will be a major change in the Spanish constitution.

French Minister of War Dies in Paris

Rumors of a Reshuffle of the Laval Cabinet

Reuters, Paris, 7th. French Minister of War Maginot died of illness today at the age of fifty-four. Maginot joined the army at the beginning of the European War, repeatedly distinguished himself in battle, and was outstanding in talent and strategy. He soon entered the cabinet and has held important government positions seven times from the European War to the present day. It is not yet determined who will succeed him.

Havas, Paris, 7th. After the death of Minister of War Maginot, several newspapers have speculated about Briand's ability to attend various international conferences, saying that the cabinet may be reshuffled, and Premier Laval may concurrently serve as Minister of Foreign Affairs. A certain member of parliament said that Laval would rather have the entire cabinet resign than reshuffle. In short, whether or not there will be a reshuffle depends on the health of Foreign Minister Briand.

European Four-Nation Economic Alliance

Aborted Due to German and Italian Opposition

Guomin, Prague, 6th. France previously intended to combine Czechoslovakia, Austria, and Hungary to form a Southeast European Economic Alliance. According to reports from Paris, this move has been aborted due to strong opposition from Germany, Italy, and Yugoslavia.

US Bank Corporation Releases Annual Silver Market Report

Reuters, New York, 5th - The American Handy & Harman Company released its annual silver market report, expressing no sympathy for artificial efforts to raise silver prices. However, it speculated that silver prices do have reasons for gradual improvement due to economic factors: 1. World silver production has significantly decreased. 2. Sales of silver coins have decreased. 3. The Indian government will no longer sell silver as there is no need to do so. 4. There are already those purchasing silver to mint coins, indicating an increasing use of silver for coinage. 5. Silver remains popular in China and India, showing no signs of decline. The report estimates that world silver production decreased by 20% in 1931, totaling 196.1 million ounces, including 88.9 million ounces from Mexico, 31.4 million ounces from the United States, 20 million ounces from Canada, 19.7 million ounces from South America (mostly Peru), and 35.7 million ounces from other locations. In 1931, the silver sold by various governments and recovered from destroyed coins saw a decrease in supply of 12 million ounces compared to 1930. Siam's destruction of silver coins increased the silver supply by 20 million ounces, while the Mexican and Indian governments sold 4.5 million ounces and 3.1 million ounces respectively. In total, excluding silver mine production, this aspect of the supply amounted to 59.5 million ounces. Since Britain abandoned the gold standard, the Indian government no longer needs to sell silver. Previously, silver sales were almost necessary to maintain the statutory gold exchange rate of the rupee. Now, there is temporarily no need to sell silver. Last year, due to political instability and sluggish commerce in India, and low prices of exported goods, India's silver consumption was only 17.7 million ounces, a 40% decrease compared to the previous year. China, including Hong Kong, saw a 52% decrease in silver consumption last year, consuming only about 59 million ounces. The total world silver consumption in 1931 was 255.6 million ounces, distributed as follows: India 57,000,000, China 59,000,000, Germany 28,000,000, United States (arts and industry) 30,000,000, England (arts and industry) 10,000,000, Mexico (arts and industry) 1,000,

000, United States (coinage) 2,400,000, consumption that could not be investigated, half of it exists in New York, London, India and other places 67,500,000, and the total world consumption is 255,600,000 ounces.

Important News

The Fall of Jinzhou in Detail

Japanese troops continue westward after occupying Jinzhou

Expected to extend to Shanhaiguan

Tianjin Correspondence - Since the establishment of the Republic of China, no year has passed without internal warfare. However, what causes us the most pain and indignation is the complete loss of the Northeast to Japan at the beginning of this year. As a reporter residing in Tianjin, I have been in contact with people from the Northeast and witnessed the atrocities of the Japanese army. The impressions I have gained are especially profound, and contemplating them fills me with tears. I will now briefly report the details of the fall of Jinzhou to the readers. The Japanese army's desire to obtain Jinzhou, overthrow our Liaoning Provisional Government, and topple Zhang Xueliang has been brewing for more than a day. Taking advantage of the Nanjing unified government's initial organization and undetermined diplomatic policies, they used their full strength to attack us, leading the League of Nations to believe that our national foundation was unstable, reducing the impact of our appeals. Indeed, the international community's reaction after this event was not as shocked and concerned as in the previous two incidents, which is regrettable. The Japanese forces attacking Jinzhou were divided into three routes advancing simultaneously: one route departed from Shenyang along the Beining Railway, facing our army head-on; one route departed from Tongliao along the Datong branch line, attacking our army's left flank; and one route departed from Yingkou along the Yinggou branch line, attacking our army's right flank. The total number of troops was approximately 20,000. In addition, they increased naval vessels and troops in Shanhaiguan and Qinhuangdao, intending to cut off our army's retreat and rear supply lines. They also conducted demonstrations in Tianjin, holding live-fire exercises in the Dongjuzi area to contain our military assistance to Jinzhou. Their arrangements were meticulous and comprehensive, while we had no preparations whatsoever. In comparison, the outcome was immediately decided. The Japanese army's plan to attack Jinzhou focused on the Yinggou branch line, as it could advance west to Goubangzi, then to the Daling River, and finally to Jinzhou. The other two routes were only intended to restrain our army from moving and redeploying. Therefore, after the Japanese army advanced from Yingkou and occupied Tianzhuangtai, they successively captured Dawa, Panshan, Hujiawopu, and Goubangzi, connecting with the Japanese army on the Beining Railway advancing from the front. Each time the Japanese army advanced, they first used large numbers of airplanes to randomly drop bombs in front to disturb our army's morale, followed by tanks and armored vehicles rushing forward with intense artillery fire to guide the infantry's assault. Our side only had volunteer soldiers and armored vehicles defending along the way, so how could they resist? In a few days, the entire Yinggou line was seized by the Japanese army. After Goubangzi fell, they further threatened Jinzhou. Therefore, Rong Zhen, the chief of staff of the Border Defense Commissioner's Office, immediately went to Ping from Jin to consult Zhang Xueliang on how to handle the situation. On the 29th of last month, he returned to Jin overnight and decided to order the troops stationed around Jinzhou to retreat into the Pass. Starting on the morning of the 30th, they began to cover the retreat of the frontline troops towards the rear. The 12th Brigade of Zhang Tingchu retreated to Zizhou, the 19th Brigade of Sun Dequan retreated to Changli, the 20th Brigade of Chang Jiwu retreated to Qian'an, the logistics training team retreated to Tangshan, and the 13th Artillery Regiment, the 1st Independent Engineer Battalion, and the Signals Battalion also retreated to Zizhou. The three cavalry brigades of Guo Xipeng, Zhang Shusen, and Bai Fengxiang, defending Dahu Mountain, detoured through Yixian along the Datong branch line and advanced towards Jiulongkou. The three cavalry detachments under the Police Department also retreated to Zizhou. Rong Zhen himself led the personnel of the Border Defense Commissioner's Office in two trains into the Pass on the evening of the 31st, arriving in Zizhou on the 1st. The Jinzhou provincial government officials also came along in the train, leaving only Huang Xiansheng in Jin to handle the administrative affairs of the provincial government. By the 1st of this month, the evacuation was complete. The Japanese army learned of our army's retreat and combined the forces from the front and sides to advance westward. It is said that the troops included the Domon Division and the Kamamura Brigade. On the 1st, they engaged in a fierce battle with our army's rearguard forces in the Daling River area. The coastal defense training army commanded by our 19th Brigade bore the brunt and was completely defeated. The machine gun companies of the 654th and 655th Regiments also suffered more than half of their casualties. Our 3rd Cavalry Brigade and 20th Infantry Brigade were separated by the main force of the Domon Division, unable to communicate with each other, and also suffered heavy losses. At the same time, the Japanese side also dropped over a hundred bombs on Jinzhou from airplanes. Our army was greatly pressured and retreated to Yunshan Station. On the afternoon of the 2nd, the Japanese army captured Jinzhou. It is reported that the vanguard of the Japanese forces, the Murashima and Murai Brigades, first entered the city from the east gate. Our security team and volunteer soldiers, at the request of the Chamber of Commerce, also withdrew from the north gate. After the Japanese army arrived in Jinzhou, they searched everywhere for Huang Xiansheng but could not find him because Huang had already left the city. Now, after occupying Jinzhou, the Japanese army has continued to advance westward in the past two days, occupying Lianshan. It is rumored that they plan to extend to Shanhaiguan by today or tomorrow to complete their long-planned work. (January 5th)

Telegram from Zhang Xueliang Before the Fall of Jinzhou Requesting Assistance

Urging the National Government to Allocate a Large Batch of Ammunition and Funds

Must Be Delivered Within a Week

Otherwise, Even a Skilled Woman Cannot Cook Without Rice

Ping News - The Intelligence Office of the Peiping Pacification Headquarters released telegrams between Zhang Xueliang and the National Government: "The Japanese army is using the forces of two divisions and six mixed brigades in a long drive to attack Jinzhou. Deputy Zhang has repeatedly telegraphed the central government since the 25th of last month, requesting ammunition and funds, as well as requesting the dispatch of reinforcements to defend to the death. Although the central government has repeatedly instructed the relevant departments to allocate funds immediately, nothing has materialized. Here are excerpts from the exchange of telegrams: 1. Deputy Zhang's Telegram to the Chairman of the Nanjing National Government, You Yin: The Japanese army has launched a large-scale westward advance, starting on the horse day. The northern route is attacking Faku to spy on Chuanwu, which our security team and reinforcements have been vigorously resisting, suffering many casualties and being forced to withdraw from Faku. The southern route is attacking Tianzhuangtai from Yingkou. Our armored vehicles and Japanese armored vehicles are in fierce conflict. The Japanese side suddenly increased a large number of cavalry and infantry, launching a fierce attack on both sides of our armored vehicles. After our strenuous efforts and reinforcements, a fierce battle ensued, resulting in many casualties, and Tianzhuangtai was eventually occupied. Our army is still gathering at the station, trying to recover it. Although the central route along the Beining Railway has not yet actively advanced, their troops concentrated in Xinmin are estimated to be over one division, and they are expected to launch a fierce westward attack within one or two days. The number of their troops stationed in Shenyang and its affiliated areas, ready to provide support at any time, is even greater. The situation is urgent, and I have repeatedly ordered the various frontline units to be strictly on guard. However, with our troops in one corner of the Northeast, facing the full strength of a powerful neighbor, the disparity in strength is too great. No matter how much we try to boost morale, we will inevitably fail. Moreover, west of Jin County, places like Qinhuangdao, Tanggu, and Tianjin are located on the coast with open gateways. Once there is a conflict in the Jin County area, they will simultaneously use naval forces to threaten our rear and disrupt Pingjin, making it difficult for us to attend to both ends. This is confirmed by the report received yesterday that three Japanese troop transport ships have entered Tanggu, indicating that this prediction is certainly correct. We will inevitably fail to attend to both ends, and since our base in the Northeast has been completely lost, we are experiencing a severe shortage of guns, cannons, ammunition, and medicine. Any attempt to sustain ourselves will be difficult. As for funding, there is even less of a solution. Our income here is already insufficient for peacetime expenses, let alone the enormous wartime needs. The officers and soldiers here are extremely indignant at the Japanese atrocities, but at this time of freezing weather, their winter uniforms are not yet complete, and the chilling cold is heartbreaking to speak of. I hope you will consider all these difficult circumstances. I have a duty and have dedicated myself to the country, so I am not afraid of hardship. However, I dare not avoid speaking about what is beyond my ability, lest it mislead the overall situation. I beg you to understand my foolish sincerity, see the truth, and immediately order the allocation of one million yuan in cash to meet the current needs for food and pay. I also know that the central government's finances are also difficult, but I must ask for the soldiers to be fed and clothed. Please also quickly allocate 16 million rounds of ammunition of a certain caliber, 8 million rounds of another caliber, 10,000 rounds of heavy artillery shells of a certain type, 70,000 rounds of field artillery shells of a certain type, 30,000 rounds of another type of field artillery shells, 80,000 rounds of field artillery shells of a certain type, 30,000 rounds of mountain artillery shells of a certain type, 230,000 rounds of mortar shells of a certain inch, and 10,000 rifles. All ammunition and funds must be delivered within a week, and the ammunition is needed most urgently, so please allocate it within the day. If rifles are inconvenient to allocate immediately, it can be delayed slightly. At the same time, please dispatch a large number of reinforcements to strengthen our forces and aid in defense. Otherwise, even a skilled woman cannot cook without rice, and even if I exhaust my foolish sincerity, it will be of no avail. The situation is urgent and cannot be delayed. My frank and direct communication is not intentional. I anxiously await your orders. Zhang Xueliang, You Yin, Secret Seal. 2. The National Government's reply to Zhang, You Dian, limited to immediate arrival: To Director Zhang, Hanqing, You Yin Dian received. The government has secretly ordered the finance, military, and staff departments to quickly raise and issue funds, and has also sent them to the Special Diplomatic Committee. Special reply, National Government, You Seal. 3. Deputy Zhang's telegram to the National Government, You You Dian, Nanjing National Government Junjian, received You Dian with respect, will make every effort to defend Jin. However, the Japanese army is using the power of the entire country, while we have only the troops of one corner. They have sufficient military supplies and sophisticated equipment, and are launching a large-scale invasion by land and air. We are undernourished and lack both equipment and ammunition. We have no preparations for air defense or cold weather. The disparity in strength is too great. I hope that you will understand all these circumstances. Once the war begins, it will not be resolved overnight. As for replenishment and reinforcements, there must be concrete measures to ensure that Japan in Tianjin has now assembled a large army. Once the battle in Jin begins, the entire situation in North China will be affected at the same time. You must plan in advance for this point, otherwise, empty words of defense will be difficult to put into practice. My officers and soldiers have the determination to sacrifice themselves, but the matter concerns the entire country, and I fear that it will not help to alleviate the difficulties. Furthermore, the aftermath problems must be planned in advance. I am duty-bound to pledge my efforts and sacrifices, and I am not afraid of any difficulties in the face of this great disaster. However, I believe that this matter is of great importance and concerns the survival of the entire country. I cannot but state the facts truthfully and ask how to deal with it. I respectfully request that you coordinate the overall situation and give concrete instructions. Zhang Xueliang, You You Yin. 4. The National Government's Civil Affairs Office's reply to Zhang, Jian Dian, limited to immediate arrival, To Director Zhang, Hanqing, Director of the Peiping Pacification Headquarters, Jian Dian received and has been forwarded to the Staff and Military Affairs Departments for review. By order, the Civil Affairs Office of the National Government, Jian Yin. 5. Deputy Zhang's urgent telegram to the Chairman of the National Government, Kan Xu Dian, very urgent, limited to immediate arrival: To the Chairman of the Nanjing National Government, Junjian, in order to defend Jin County, I requested the allocation of funds and ammunition. I then received a telegram stating that the relevant departments had been instructed to handle it separately, showing your concern for the border and your intention to protect the country and the people. However, the Japanese army has been pressing closer and closer, and Jin County is in extreme danger. Our army is determined to resist to the death, and the enemy has not yet succeeded. However, although the morale is strong, we lack both funds and ammunition. If the enemy launches a large-scale advance, even if all the soldiers in the Northeast are sacrificed, it will be difficult to defend. The matter concerns the entire country, and since you have repeatedly ordered them to fulfill their duties, you should provide practical support. The matter is urgent, and I hope that you will still look into the previous telegram and quickly order the relevant departments to allocate funds as soon as possible to meet the immediate needs. I urgently await your orders. Zhang Xueliang, Kan Yin. 6. The Civil Affairs Office of the Nanjing National Government's reply to Zhang, Yan You Dian, limited to immediate arrival: To Director Zhang, Hanqing, Director of the Peiping Pacification Headquarters, Junjian, the matters stated in Kan Secret Dian have been properly and confidentially forwarded to the relevant departments for prompt handling. Special reply, the Civil Affairs Office of the National Government, Yan You Yin."

White Russians Still Active in Harbin

Has Become a Dispute Between White Russians and the Police

The North China Daily News, Harbin, 5th - Although the police authorities used firm measures at the end of the week to deal with the disputes between White Russians and Chinese people, order in Harbin has not been fully restored. Last night, there were many gunshots again, and rioters attacked the police, causing the police to fire in six places to suppress them. As a result, no rioters were killed or injured, but one policeman was killed and two were injured. It is now clear that this has become a problem between White Russians and the police. The Soviet Consul-General has notified the Chinese authorities that if any of the rioters arrested claim to be Soviet citizens, he hopes that they will be severely punished.

Second Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Party Headquarters

Resolution to Retain Wu Chao-chu as President of the Judicial Yuan

The Second Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Executive Committee of the Kuomintang was held at 8:00 AM on the 7th in the First Conference Hall. Attendees included Ye Chucang, Sun Ke, Yu Youren, Ju Zheng, and Chen Guofu. Observers included Deng Jiayan, Huang Jichen, Lin Sen, Chen Mingshu, Yang Jie, Miao Peicheng, Gu Zhutong, Bai Yunti, Zhang Renjie, Zhang Huichang, Ma Chaojun, Ji Liang, Wang Qi, Li Ciwen, He Yingqin, Liang Hancao, Li Wenfan, Zhao Pilian, Huang Musong, Li Zonghuang, Shi Qingyang, Hong Ludong, Zhu Peide, Gu Zhenggang, Deng Feihuang, Guo Chuntao, Yu Jingtang, Shao Lizi, Duan Xipeng, Xie Zuomin, Xiao Jishan, Kexinge, Luo Jialun, Zhang Lisheng, Fang Juehui, Liu Shouzhong, Chen Gongbo, Qin Zhen, Zhang Zhiben, and Fan Yusui. Ju Zheng chaired the meeting, and Ye Chucang served as the secretary-general. The following resolutions were passed: 1. Regarding Committee Member Wu Chao-chu's request to resign as the President of the Judicial Yuan, it was resolved to retain him. Before his arrival at the Yuan, the Vice-President will act on his behalf according to the law. 2. Regarding Committee Member Shao Yuan-chong's request to resign as the Standing Committee Member of the Party History Compilation Committee, it was resolved to retain him. 3. The Reception Center for Students Returning from Russia will be transferred to the Mass Movement Guidance Committee. 4. Regarding the letter from the Central Supervisory Committee concerning the detailed provisions of Article 3 of the Rules for the Review of Party Affairs by Supervisory Committees or Supervisory Committee Members at all levels, which is inconsistent with the current organization of Party Headquarters in various provinces, cities, and counties, the Fifth Plenary Meeting resolved to delete the words "various departments, offices, and committees" in Article 3 and requested that the amendment be checked and announced. The resolution was approved. 5. Regarding the letter from the Central Supervisory Committee concerning the detailed provisions of Articles 3 and 4 of the Procedures for Auditing Finances by Supervisory Committees at all levels, which is inconsistent with the organization of Party Headquarters in various provinces, counties, and cities, the Fifth Plenary Meeting resolved to delete Article 3 and amend Article 4 to read: "The income and expenditure of various organs affiliated with the Executive Committee at all levels shall be submitted by the Executive Committee at that level to the Supervisory Committee or Supervisory Committee Member at that level for auditing." The amendment, along with the original text, was requested to be checked and announced. The resolution was approved. 6. The Central Supervisory Committee submitted four cases of disciplinary action against Party members. Yang Tingjie (stationed in Japan) was expelled from the Party, as were Weng Hui (Zhejiang Xu Yun), Xu Yiren (Zhejiang Shaoxing), and Yang Shilu (Zhejiang Xiaoshan) for one year, one year, and six months, respectively. All resolutions were approved. 7. Committee Member Chen Mingshu was nominated to present a report at next Monday's Central Memorial Week.

Establishment of the Hunan National Crisis Relief Association

The Hunan National Crisis Relief Association held its inaugural meeting in Changsha on December 27th and issued the following declaration: "In today's world, it is unheard of for a nation not to rise up in self-defense when facing a national crisis, nor is it heard of to rely solely on diplomatic solutions when the enemy is deeply entrenched. It is especially unheard of to lack appropriate decision-making in both peace and war, and to merely delay the situation, passively accepting encroachment. The shame of Japan's occupation of our Eastern Provinces has reached this extreme. The League of Nations' assistance has already been disappointing, and the government officials are only engaging in disputes. At this time when the nation's fate hangs by a thread, if we do not strengthen our forces and urge the Party and national officials to quickly form a capable government, then preparations for war will be empty words. However, there are myriad ways to support the weak and reverse the situation, but to defend against insult and save the nation, the people must first unite. The people of Hunan have sacrificed much in the revolution. Although we dare not be the first to claim credit, we certainly do not want to lag behind in rushing to righteousness. We now follow the example of the gentlemen in Jiangsu and Zhejiang in organizing the National Crisis Relief Association, focusing our efforts internally to urge the government to quickly resolve the disputes between the Party and the government, and externally to unite our will to resist the strong neighbor and reject compromises that cede our rights. Once the national crisis is over, the Association will cease its activities. We hereby encourage each other and make this declaration."

At the same time, a public telegram was sent to the Nanjing government as follows: "To the Executive Committee of the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, the Chairman of the National Government, the Presidents of the Executive, Legislative, Judicial, Supervisory, and Examination Yuans, and all Ministers Junjian, since Japan sent troops to invade and occupy the Eastern Provinces, the whole country has been shocked. Seeking solutions through diplomacy, the League of Nations meetings have repeatedly teetered on failure. Attempting to revitalize through internal affairs, the disputes between Beijing and Guangdong are merely wasting time. The great disaster is imminent, and public sentiment is increasingly anxious. Recently, the Japanese army has further attacked Jinzhou and harassed Jin-Yu. Our country is unprepared for both peace and war. Looking back at the key figures in the Party and government, they are still mired in political struggles, suspecting each other, either recuperating at sea or retiring to their hometowns. The central government is merely undergoing changes, with no decisions being made to resist insult. The deterioration of the situation to this point is alarming. As citizens of Hunan, can we turn a blind eye to the nation entrusted to our lives and not seek relief as it falls into ruin? We believe that our country has been advocating Party rule for five years now. The people earnestly desire governance and are holding their breath to listen to political tutelage. However, the actual results achieved in recent years are quite the opposite. Internal strife is endless, and disasters are spreading, making life difficult for the people, threatening the nation itself. Now that a strong neighbor is pressing us, and we have lost three provinces in less than a month, the Party and government officials who hold important positions still do not feel the seriousness of the situation and the magnitude of their responsibilities. There is no expression of sorrow or self-blame, no spirit of sacrifice and unity. Is this what the mission of Party rule is like? If the nation is not preserved, where will the Party be attached? Those who gain the right people will prosper, and those who lose them will perish. May our Party and government officials reflect deeply on this. The only way to counter the outside is to unite the country, and the only way to stabilize the inside is through open politics. There is no shortage of enlightened people among the Party and government officials. They should abandon their past grievances, dissolve their prejudices, adopt a selfless and patriotic attitude, and treat the people with sincerity. Now that a unified government has been formed, it should take responsibility and quickly dispatch troops to rescue the Northeast and save the people from fire and water. Moreover, in the spirit of the Prime Minister's ideal of 'serving the world selflessly', it should immediately convene a national conference and formulate a constitution, so that we can stabilize the inside, repel the outside, and bring a fresh start. The people's hearts can be solidified, and the national crisis can be averted. We are alarmed and write in haste. We hope that you will consider this. Zhao Qilin, Xiong Xiling, Qin Bingzhi, Shen Kegang, Wang Yishu, Zhao Hengti, Guo Zongxi, Cheng Songwan, Huang Fengqi, Zheng Yuan, Peng Yunyi, Nie Qijie, Fan Rui, Cheng Zikai, Xia Shoutian, Peng Qingli, Chen Jiayan, Luo Xiankai, Chen Binsheng, Xiao Du, Fu Shaofei, Cheng Chongxin, Zhang Hongquan, Liang Huanyi, Hu Yuantan, Wang Shouchi, Ren Fuli, Chen Runlin, Xiong Zongxu, Fang Kegang, Shi Yi, Fu Yonglin, Gu Tianyou, Liao Yi, and Xie Guozhao of the Hunan National Crisis Relief Association, together kowtow, Jiang."

Summary of Important News

Han Fuqu Consolidates Security in Shandong Province

Taking Preventive Measures Against Japanese Disruptions

Jinan Correspondence: Provincial Chairman Han Fuqu, considering the fall of Jinzhou and the increasingly tense situation in North China, and recognizing Shandong's crucial position connecting the north and south, along with the unpredictable appearance of Japanese warships at Qingdao, Yantai, and Longkou ports, and the large number of Japanese residents in Jinan, which could easily lead to pretexts for trouble, convened a meeting on the morning of the fourth. Attending were all committee members, department heads, Jinan Mayor Wen Chenglie, Garrison Commander Lei Taiping, Public Security Bureau Chief Wang Kairu, and others to discuss countermeasures. It was resolved that: 1) Regardless of how the situation changes, the decision is to protect the region, ensure the safety of the people, and maintain security in the province; 2) Regarding finances, if the Third Route Army's military pay cannot be issued by the central government, it will be temporarily borrowed from the central government's tax revenue within the province to maintain operations, without increasing the burden on the people. There will be no changes to personnel in various tax collection agencies; 3) Regarding education, schools had previously started winter vacation early due to student unrest. Recently, students from various schools have requested an early start to the semester, showing a commendable eagerness to study. It was decided that the semester will begin on February 1st as scheduled, without further delay. The meeting adjourned around 10 AM. At that time, Song Shiyan, the military education corps leader sent by Han Fuqu to Beiping last month, happened to return to Jinan from Beiping after meeting with Zhang. He immediately went to the provincial government to report to Han, stating that Zhang Xueliang would jointly maintain security in North China with Han, and various North China generals had arrived in Beiping to meet with Zhang. Zhang plans to send Wan Fulin to Jinan within a day or two to discuss everything and deal with the difficult situation together.

In recent days, Japanese residents in Qingdao have repeatedly attempted to cause trouble, with the navy repeatedly landing to demonstrate, causing anxiety among the people. Han Fuqu, recognizing Qingdao as the terminus of the railway, which is crucial to Shandong's transportation, and fearing that villains and bandits might be exploited, ordered Rong Guangxing, the brigade commander of the 87th Brigade of the 29th Division stationed in Jiaoxian, on the 30th of last month to strengthen vigilance, to prevent problems before they arise. He also ordered Dai Hongbin, commander of the railway artillery, and Zhang Tingxian, the second team leader, to take the Taishan armored vehicle and all soldiers, fully armed, and with tools such as shovels, to patrol the Jiaozhou area. He also telegraphed Qingdao Mayor and Navy Commander Shen Honglie to coordinate defense with Rong Guangxing's troops to ensure complete security. (4th)

Han Fuqu Sends Song Shiyan to Beiping

Jinan Correspondence: The Shandong Provincial Government, after Zhang Xueliang, Director of the Beiping Pacification Headquarters, telegraphed an invitation to Han Fuqu to visit Beiping, which he was unable to accept personally, specially sent Song Shiyan, head of the Third Route Army Military Education Corps, as his representative to discuss security and financial issues in North China. He returned yesterday (the 4th) after completing his mission and reported to Han on his meeting with Zhang and Zhang's views on security in North China. Han, recently concerned about the loss of Jinzhou, the increasingly urgent diplomatic situation, and the critical importance of security in North China, urgently needs to send someone to be stationed in Beiping to facilitate contact whenever issues arise. Therefore, he dispatched Song Shiyan to Beiping again. After receiving the order, Song left Jinan for the north on the Pingpu train this afternoon (the 5th). According to Song, Chairman Han believes that with the current urgent diplomatic situation and the importance of security in North China, although Zhang Xueliang has resigned from his position as deputy commander, he must still bear the responsibility for security in North China. Shandong is a part of North China, and there must be personnel stationed in Beiping to facilitate contact whenever issues arise. Therefore, Chairman Han specially sent Shiyan as his representative to Beiping. Currently, Deputy Commander Zhang and the generals and constitutionalists in North China are extremely united. As for the issue of Shandong Province, it must follow the lead of the central government. How it will be resolved in the future, I cannot judge. (5th)

Huangpi County, Hubei Province, Again in Grave Danger

Fellow Provincials in Hankou Request Pacification Headquarters to Dispatch Large Forces for Urgent Suppression

To Secure Wuhan's Defenses and Protect the Pinghan Railway

Hankou Correspondence: The Red bandit Kuang Jixun's troops in Hubei Province, with a total of tens of thousands from the 11th, 12th, 13th Divisions and the Independent 4th Brigade, recently captured Huang'an County. Zhao Guanying's 69th Division suffered heavy losses. The authorities have only now become aware of the rampant banditry and are mobilizing troops to suppress them vigorously. Unexpectedly, after the bandits occupied Huang'an, they gradually invaded westward, and the bandits in the northern border of Huangpi also took the opportunity to stir up trouble, putting the county seat in imminent danger. The county borders Hankou and the Pinghan Railway runs directly through it, making its strategic importance extremely important. The garrison force is considered rather weak. He Chengjun, Director of the Pacification Headquarters, and Li Mingzhong, Pacification Supervisor of the Henan-Anhui-Hubei Border Area, are deeply concerned about this and have reportedly increased the number of troops sent to intercept them. The situation of Huangpi's northern border being ravaged by bandits and the danger of the county seat has been reported in detail by fellow provincials in Hankou to Director He via telegram, and they have also telegraphed Minister He of the Military and Political Department, requesting him to thoroughly suppress the bandits to save the people in distress, consolidate Wuhan's defenses, and ensure the safety of the Pinghan Railway. The original telegram reads: "The banditry in Huangpi is deepening daily, and the Red bandits have approached Wuhan. Now, for the sake of consolidating Wuhan's defenses, ensuring the safety of the southern section of the Pinghan Railway, facilitating the suppression of the Red bandits in eastern Hubei, and urgently saving the lives of the people, we earnestly request the urgent dispatch of large forces to vigorously carry out suppression. The pressing situation is hereby presented in detail. Huangpi is bordered by Hankou City to the south, Luoshan, Henan to the north, the southern section of the Pinghan Road to the west, and the old nest of the Red bandits in Huang'an to the east. For years, the northern part has been ravaged by bandits, and the number of people slaughtered, houses burned, and women raped is countless. Last year, the southern part also suffered from floods. The county residents who have not died from weapons and floods are in a state of displacement, poverty, and disease. There are now over ten thousand people displaced and destitute with nowhere to turn. If they are not rescued, they will either die, flee, or surrender to the Red bandits. This is why we must urgently save the lives of the people and earnestly request the urgent dispatch of large forces for suppression. First. The Red bandits have long threatened to invade Wuhan, and it is within expectations that they will take advantage of any changes in the situation to invade. Currently, the bandit forces in Hubei are strongest in eastern Hubei and Jiangbei. Those planning to attack Wuhan will definitely use the bandits in eastern Hubei as their main force, with Huangpi as the only route of passage. Therefore, for years, the Red bandits have always taken extremely slow and meticulous measures in Huangpi, gradually Redifying the south. The local people initially resisted, then fled, and finally succumbed, truly unable to extricate themselves. Huang'an was lost again last month. In central Huangpi, Paojiawan and Tianjiawan, which could be defended, have been gradually captured by the bandits. There are no more villages or fortresses that can be defended further south. Only the county seat is not a stronghold that can stop the bandits from advancing south. If the bandits invade south of the county seat, they can invade Hankou City along the railway, the lake road, or the river road. There are no longer any dangerous passes that are easy to defend in between. Moreover, most of the residents in Wuhan City are from Huangpi, with over ten thousand normally, and over twenty thousand at this time. Their traffic is frequent. In addition to cars, ships, and pedestrians, the railway must also open a short-ticket train once a day. If the people of Huangpi are banditized, there will be no way to cut off their traffic militarily and carry out inspections and prevention. This is why we must consolidate Wuhan's defenses and earnestly request the urgent dispatch of large forces for suppression. Second. The southern section of the Pinghan Railway runs parallel to the territory of Huangpi. The stations south of Wushengguan, Guangshui, and Huayuan are not within Huangpi, but they are connected to the county. The distance is only a few dozen miles. Last year, the Red bandits who attacked the troops of Dai, Guo, Qian, Peng Brigade, and Yue in the Huayuan area used the mountains bordering Huangpi and Xiaogan as their nest. Now that the northern part of Huangpi has fallen into the bandit area, the southern section of the Pinghan Railway can be destroyed at any time. This is why we must ensure the safety of the southern section of the Pinghan Railway and earnestly request the urgent dispatch of large forces for suppression. Third. Huangpi is connected to Luoshan in the north, which is the most important place for large Red bandit forces in the Hubei-Henan border area to invade south. Whether defending or suppressing the large Red bandit forces in eastern Hubei, we should start from Huangpi and advance eastward. After the Huangpi area is cleared, it can cut off the connection between the Red bandits in eastern Hubei and northern Hubei. Furthermore, it is easy to divide troops and search eastward by using the convenience of the railway stations along the Pinghan Railway to mobilize troops. This is why we must facilitate the suppression of the large Red bandit forces in eastern Hubei and earnestly request the urgent dispatch of large forces for suppression. Fourth. However, for the past three or four years, there has never been a case of using Huangpi as a base and dispatching large forces eastward from the stations along the Pinghan Road for search and suppression. During the division of jurisdictions in the 17th and 18th years, the eastern Hubei region was limited to the counties under the old Huangzhou Prefecture, and the Huangpi pacification affairs were only concurrently managed by the Wuhan Northern District Fortress Command. However, the fortress's troops could not reach far, resulting in the abandonment of areas in the northern countryside directly bordering Henan, with no one responsible for their safety, allowing the bandit forces to grow. In the past one or two years, due to frequent troop transfers, there has been little vigorous search and suppression. The bandits in the northern countryside originally had the ability to destroy the Pinghan traffic at any time, but judging from their intentions, except for the opportunity to attack military troops and seize weapons, they do not often disturb the railway, fearing that it will attract the government's attention and lead to the addition of large forces for suppression. The government has indeed seemed to neglect this point and has not paid much attention to it, resulting in the bandit forces invading southwards and approaching Wuhan, which is extremely worrying. Based on the above, we dare to make an urgent plea and earnestly request review and approval." (January 6th)

Guangchang in Jiangxi Province Captured by Bandits Again

Nanchang Correspondence: Guangchang is located north of Shicheng and Ningdu, south of Nanfeng, connected to Yongfeng and Le'an in the west, and bordering Jianning and Taining in Fujian to the east. The area is mountainous and transportation is extremely inconvenient. It was originally one of Zhu and Mao's base areas in eastern Jiangxi. In August of last year, it was once recovered by various armies, and the general headquarters established a party and government district branch in the county seat to handle all post-war affairs. Later, after Zhu and Mao's main forces fled from Xingguo to Shicheng, Huichang, and Jianning and Ninghua in Fujian, Guangchang and Ningdu were again invaded by the Red bandits. At the beginning of December, the civil defense corps in various places in Huichang and Shicheng were successively attacked and destroyed by the bandits, and Huichang City was also captured. At that time, the Guangdong army was only lingering on the Jiangxi-Guangdong border, and the 26th Route Army and the 6th Route Army were exhausted from prolonged fighting and could only hold their respective county seats. Therefore, Zhu and Mao launched a large-scale eastern offensive. According to news from Nanfeng, Zhu and Mao's pseudo 4th and 7th armies attacked Guangchang from Shicheng. The troops stationed in the city retreated to Nanfeng and Nancheng. As a result, Guangchang County was captured by Zhu and Mao again on December 15th. Nanfeng is also quite strained and has repeatedly telegraphed the Pacification Headquarters for troops. At the same time, Ganzhou sent an urgent telegram because Xingguo and Yudu had fallen to the bandits. It is heard that the newly appointed Pacification Director Zhu Shaoliang is determined to reinvigorate the spirit and actively suppress the Red bandits, and plans to order the front-line armies to change from defense to offense, and order the units of Mao Bingwen, Sun Lianzhong, and Xu Kexiang to dare to recover the lost territory within the shortest period of time to avoid irreparable consequences.

The Current Situation in Wuyuan After the Bandits Retreated

Wuyuan Correspondence: The Jiangxi Communist bandits led by Zhou Tang and others captured Wuyuan City on the morning of December 17th and plundered wealth. The next morning, they retreated towards Dexing. The main cadres with firearms did not stay in Dexing but fled directly to their base in Guixi. Those with spears and local communists are still hiding in the Dexing-Wuyuan border area. After receiving reports from fellow provincials in Jingde and Wuyuan, Commander Ruan stationed in Leping immediately telegraphed and ordered Brigade Commander Zhang stationed in Dexing to lead his two regiments, Wu and Wang, to encircle Wuyuan's southern Taibai from Dexing. He also sent Han Changchuan's battalion to Wuyuan for defense. Commander Ruan personally went to Taibai to direct the pursuit. The Yuehe First Ship Inspection Bureau established by the bandits in Tongbu has been destroyed, and the bandit areas in Jiaotian and Wangcun in southern Dexing have also been thoroughly suppressed to eradicate the roots. Initially, the county seat's security was precarious because no one was responsible for county affairs. The county's Chamber of Commerce, Tea Guild, and various organizations jointly formed a temporary Security and Post-Disaster Committee, electing Dong Jifu, Cheng Wenwu, and nine others as committee members to handle post-disaster affairs. Only when the Jiangxi troops arrived in the county seat on the 22nd did the people's hearts and order gradually stabilize. Several abducted hostages have not yet been released. The Good-Will Committee learned that Wang Huayin of the Qianyuan Pharmacy was forced to pay an insufficient amount by the bandit army and was taken away, and was instructed to prepare the money to redeem him. On the 19th, they collected the money and sent someone to redeem him, but upon reaching Dexing, they did not dare to proceed due to the intense pursuit by the army along the way and returned with the money. Currently, the Good-Will Committee, to ensure the safety of each hostage, has specially requested Battalion Commander Han to issue a passport and make further efforts to redeem them. The captured Catholic priest has already been issued a telegram by the Foreign Ministry of the National Government and the provincial government, ordering the local garrison and public organizations to rescue him from danger within a time limit. Moreover, in Wuyuan City's prosperous Northwest Street, from Jichang Pawnshop to Xiguan, all major shops have suffered losses. Companies such as Dinghe Oil Shop, Runchang Lisun Cloth Shop, and China-Germany Company have decided to close down due to being completely looted. Most of the others have not yet reopened. The county elementary school has also suffered too much damage and will be difficult to reopen this year. Former County Magistrate Qi Qingchi went to Jin province before the city fell and is reportedly no longer returning to his post. The provincial government has appointed Ke Kaiwen (formerly the County Magistrate of Yingshan) to take over in Wuyuan and is expected to arrive in Wuyuan within days. However, the county government offices were burned down, and the administration has lost its place. It is generally agreed to use Ziyang Academy as the government site and a selection and deployment will be made again after the new county magistrate arrives. (December 27th)

The Second National Congress of Physicians

Many Important Motions Resolved

Hangzhou News: The Second National Congress of the National Physicians' Association was held at the Hangzhou YMCA for three days starting on New Year's Day. More than one hundred representatives from various provinces, cities, and counties and more than two hundred physicians attended. More than twenty pharmaceutical factories displayed their products at the congress, making it a grand occasion. The opening ceremony was held at 9:00 AM on New Year's Day. Chu Minyi was publicly elected as the temporary chairman. The chairman gave an opening speech, followed by speeches by Hangzhou Mayor Zhao Zhiyou and Director of the Department of Health Shu Sheng on behalf of Jin Baoshan and others. Finally, Permanent Chairman Xu Nali reported on the association's work. Chu Minyi, Sheng Peicong, Xu Nali, Wang Wanbai, Wang Qizhang, Zhang Yunhan, Chen Wenda, Chen Weitang, Qian Baohua, Hong Bairong, and Wu Xinqi were publicly elected as the eleven members of the presidium. At 1:00 PM, the entire group took a photo, and at 2:00 PM, the meeting resumed. The meeting continued on the 2nd and 3rd to discuss the motions and resolved many important matters, mostly concerning major issues such as saving the country, promoting academic research, and promoting national health. All the representatives gathered their minds for discussion and fully expressed their opinions. Finally, they also resolved to send a telegram to comfort Ma Zhanshan and elect executive and supervisory committee members. As a result, Xu Nali, Wang Qizhang, Pang Jingzhou, Niu Huisheng, Yu Yunxiu, Cai Yu, Jiang Zhenzhu, Zhu Qiluo, and Xia Shenchu were elected as executive committee members. Wang Yugang, Zhang Yunhan, and You Pengxi were elected as alternate executive committee members. Chu Minyi, Sheng Peicong, Wang Wanbai, Hong Bairong, and Mao Xian were elected as supervisory committee members. Chen Wenda and Chen Fangzhi were elected as alternate supervisory committee members. Moreover, the conference proceeded smoothly. Out of more than eighty motions, except for a few that were voluntarily withdrawn by the representatives, the remaining seventy were all thoroughly discussed and resolved in a suitable manner. Therefore, the closing ceremony was held at 5:00 PM on the afternoon of the 3rd, and the entire group dispersed after cheering "Long live!"

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Testimony of Witnesses in Tang's Murder Case: Tang Zhiqi, the owner of Tang Helong store outside the West Gate of this city, was assassinated last year. Yang Shijie, a supervising officer of the Public Security Bureau, arrested Shen Shaoqing, a habitual thief who had escaped from prison. At the prosecutor's office, Shen confessed that Tang Daguan hired two unnamed fugitives to carry out the assassination, and that he was only responsible for digging and prying open the wall. Following this, Tang Qiusheng, the son of the deceased, was suspected and summoned for questioning and prosecuted in the criminal court. On the 21st of last month, Criminal Court Judge Zhang questioned the thief Shen Shaoqing, who suddenly retracted his confession, claiming that the investigators of the Public Security Bureau had promised him a reward of 10% or 4,000 yuan, and had given him opium on the spot to teach him what to say. Now that his conscience has been awakened, he said that it has nothing to do with Tang Qiusheng. The court then issued a warrant to summon witnesses Yang Jie and others, and the court was reconvened at 9:00 AM today (the 7th) for continued questioning. The judge summoned Yang Shijie, the supervising officer of the Public Security Bureau in charge of the case, to court to question him about the case investigation. Then, Shen Shaoqing was summoned to court, and his confession was similar to the previous one, except that he changed the promised reward of forty yuan to four yuan, and added that during a certain time in the waiting room, Yang had given him one yuan, and someone wearing a red-rimmed hat had gone to exchange it for small change. The judge immediately gathered all the police officers and ordered Shen to identify them, but he was unable to do so, and said that there was another person wearing plain clothes. Yang Shijie then stated that since Shen Shaoqing's confession first mentioned someone wearing a red-rimmed hat and then changed it to someone wearing plain clothes, he asked the judge to investigate this point. Tang Qiusheng was also summoned and questioned about whether he had a good relationship with his brother Tang Jingren. Tang replied that they had a normal relationship, and the rest of his testimony was similar to his previous statement. The apprentice Ye Diankui was also questioned briefly. Tang Qiusheng's lawyer, Zhang Baopei, requested that Tang Qiusheng be released on bail. The judge ruled that the judgment in this case was imminent, and Chu will be summoned again for questioning and verification.

Post Office Embezzlement of Large Sums: At 2:00 AM on the 6th, the West Gate Post Office of this city heard noises. When the staff were awakened to check, they found that the door of the safe in the director's office had been pried open, and 2,000 yuan in cash was missing. They immediately reported it to the Public Security Bureau, which sent Supervising Officer Yang Shijie to investigate. The thief climbed down from the post office's patio using a ladder and broke open the iron safe door. When the victim became aware of the situation, the thief hurriedly took the loot and escaped through the back door. Director Gu of the post office has personally requested the Public Security Bureau to investigate and has reported it to the headquarters.

Theft of Hairtail Fishing Boat Revealed: On the 5th, a hairtail fishing boat from the Doxing Seafood Company in Caoging North Library, along with many other fishermen, arrived. However, apart from the captain, they were all pirates monitoring the situation and forbidding anyone from speaking out. They took the fish and left without paying the price. Later, the captain informed the owner of the company, Lu Zikuang, who reported it to the 15th Precinct of the town. Police Officer Wu Zongchen immediately pursued the pirates. When they arrived at the bank of the North Library Bridge, the lookout resisted arrest and fought for about half an hour. The pirates fled far away, and only a Mauser rifle, a bayonet, and two cartridge clips were recovered. Fearing that the fishing boat parked on the beach would be hijacked by the pirates, they reported it to the water police to guard it. Currently, the captain Zhang Ruishi, Zheng Xiaosheng, and Yang Derong, along with the recovered weapons, have been brought to Songjiang. According to their confession, the total value of the boat and cargo was 540 yuan. 260 yuan had already been taken by the pirates, and the remaining amount would be paid tonight. They are all victims. Officer Wu has mailed a notice to the families of the fishermen to come and collect it.

Nanhui

Shen Xengeng Sentenced to Death: Yesterday, the county government sentenced Shen Xengeng to death for the crime of killing a direct ascendant relative in the west seventh township of this county, depriving him of his civil rights for life.

Taking Evidence in Forging Signature Case: The Zhenjiang District Court previously sent a letter to the county government, requesting assistance in taking evidence in the case of Chen Shixian, former member of the County Party Rectification Committee, and others forging seals and framing comrades. Wang Dongyuan and other falsely accused party members provided testimony and sent it for review. Yesterday was the date for taking evidence. Wang Dongyuan and others testified in court that Chen Shixian and others were indeed the instigators of forging the signatures and requested a thorough investigation.

Changshu

Robbery and Murder in West Xu Market: Wang Laosan, a native of Changyinsha, Jiangbei, who was taking care of a graveyard in Yangjiaba, West Xu Market, Phoenix District of this county, lived there with his wife and daughters. He collected 300 yuan in mutual aid funds the night before. That night, Qi San, a fellow villager, came to stay overnight. Unexpectedly, two men suddenly came with knives in the middle of the night to rob. They first tied up Wang Laosan and threw a lime bag at him, but it missed. Wang resisted the robbers and was stabbed in the throat with a sharp knife, causing him to die. When Wang's wife and daughters saw this, they got up and were also beaten. Wang's second daughter escaped through the back door and reported it to the district office, which sent the security corps. The robbers had already fled, but Wang Laosan was found lying dead on the ground. When Wang's wife was questioned, she said that the mutual aid funds had been completely robbed, and that she had reported the matter of someone staying overnight the night before. The corps police went to the Qi family pier to search Qi's house, but Qi and others denied it. They only found a felt hat with the words "Chen Kerong" on it. When asked, they only said that this person lived in Gushan. They then rushed to the pavilion under Gushan Slope and captured two men, both with bloodstains on their hands and faces. They also found a small knife seven or eight inches long beside them, with bloodstains still visible. One claimed to be Chen Kerong, and the other claimed to be Chen Laosan. They brought Qi San, Zhu A'gen, and nine others to the police station and transferred them to the county government for questioning. Chen Kerong and Chen Laosan confessed to killing Wang Laosan. The others were suspected. The county government is still investigating.

Suspicious Japanese Person Ordered to Leave the Country: On the 4th, a traveler suddenly came to the Dadong Hotel outside the South Gate of this county, claiming to be Japanese and accompanied by a male servant. He was extravagant and called prostitutes for pleasure all day long. The Second Precinct of the Public Security Bureau heard about this and went to investigate. The Japanese person immediately produced a business card with the words "Member of the International League Association, Koki Sei," and "Shanghai" below it. On the back, there were nine articles, including "International Labor Organization, Establishment of the Eight-Hour Work System, Prohibition of Night Work for Women, Immigration." The police deemed him suspicious and took him to the police station. The Japanese person then claimed, "I am Japanese and not subject to Chinese interference," and immediately telegraphed the Japanese consulate in Suzhou for assistance. After detailed questioning by the Party Committee, he claimed to have been born in Japan, but his parents were both overseas Chinese. He became a Japanese citizen at the age of two, returned to China at the age of fourteen, and is now fifty-five years old. He currently resides in Suzhou and came here for travel. The Public Security Bureau, considering the matter to be of great importance, transferred him to the county government on the night of the 5th. County Magistrate Yi, together with Trial Staff Member Chai and Party Committee An Weinan, opened the court for questioning. Gao confessed as before. The county determined that Gao had no criminal suspicion. The prostitution part was handed over to the Public Security Bureau for handling. As a result, the bureau sentenced him to ten days of detention, which was later changed to a fine of ten yuan. He was released on bail and ordered to leave the country.

Police Officer Mistakenly Injures Farmer While Shooting a Dog: The citizens of Xiaozhen, Zhizhang, Zhengxiu District of this county, were in a state of panic due to the robbery by bandits in the previous year. They specially submitted a joint request to the county government, requesting to send a police team to the town for defense. The county government ordered Qian, the captain of the county police team, to allocate more than twenty police officers to the town for defense. Fortunately, they have been living in peace. Recently, the Liu Wu family in the town had a yellow dog that was used to guard the house, but it was quite fierce and liked to steal food. On the 4th of this month, the dog went to the house of Du, the captain of the police team, to steal dishes and broke many bowls. Du was very angry and tried to chase it, but the dog had already gone far. The next day, the dog was lying on the ground and was seen by a police officer. He returned to the team headquarters, obtained a rifle, loaded it with live ammunition, and rushed to the dog's location. He aimed and fired, but the dog was startled and escaped. Seeing that he was about to miss, the police officer fired a second shot at the dog. Unexpectedly, the dog escaped, and the bullet mistakenly hit the back of a farmer named Zhou Maosong. Zhou immediately fell to the ground. When Zhou's wife saw this, she rushed to the district office to report that her husband had been shot and was about to die. When District Chief Gu heard this, he immediately ordered someone to investigate. It turned out that it was a police officer who had mistakenly shot him. On one hand, he sent the injured farmer Zhou Maosong to Jishan in the city for medical treatment. On the other hand, he reported the situation to Qian Mobin, the captain of the police team, for handling. It is unknown what Captain Qian will do.

Another Shuttle Bus Added to Suzhou-Changshu Route: The traffic between Suzhou and Changshu in this county originally had the Huimin China Bus and the morning and evening buses of the China Merchants Bureau. Later, the Huimin Company stopped running due to internal disputes. Now, someone has organized the Huimin Company and added the Suzhou-Changshu bus, extending the route from Gangkou Town in Changshu to Suzhou. A wharf has also been set up in the urban area of Changshu outside the West Gate. The time is at 11:00 AM and 2:00 PM. It started running on the 5th. In response, the Huimin Bus also resumed running on the 6th, with the time still being 10:00 AM to Suzhou every morning and returning to Changshu at 3:00 PM.

Suzhou

International Inspection Team Inspects for Disease: A specialist from the International Education Inspection Team's health group, Dr. Jugg, a professor at Yale University, along with a translator and the head of the Health and Welfare Section of the Ministry of Interior, Master Yao Yongzheng, arrived in Suzhou on the 6th. On the 7th, Gao Huaizhi was dispatched by the county government to accompany them to various schools to inspect for malaria. They are scheduled to continue their inspection today (the 8th).

Western Doctor Accused of Negligence: Xu Gao, wife of Xu Jingqing, residing at No. 36 along the river street inside Chang Gate, sought medical treatment from Western doctor Yu Shengjia's clinic for a throat ailment. After Dr. Yu administered a blood serum injection, Xu Gao suddenly died. Xu Jingqing, believing Dr. Yu was negligent, apprehended Dr. Yu and brought him to the police precinct, who then transferred him to the District Procuratorate. He was released on bail after paying a 500 yuan cash deposit, pending investigation. Meanwhile, Western doctor Hui was invited to examine the cause of death.

Jiangyin

Military Department Orders Investigation into Wei Dacheng's Inspection of British Ship: Wei Dacheng, the former chief inspector of the fortress, along with Han Bangzun, Hu Yimin, Hu Peize, and others, attempted to inspect the Tai Gu Company's Wuhu ship at the port on December 25th of last year. They were detained by a British warship and handed over to the provincial government for handling. The provincial government has already sent a letter to the Ministry of Military Affairs to handle the case. The military department sent a section member to Cheng to investigate the fortress headquarters and inquire about everything in detail, returning to Beijing at the end of the year. Commander Yang also personally went to Beijing a few days ago to report the details to the Ministry of Military Affairs. Since Wei Dacheng was only an inspector in the Joint Defense Sheng in the spring and had already been dismissed, the Ministry of Military Affairs is still thoroughly investigating whether he impersonated an official.

Nantong

Relief Wheat Transported and Distributed to Disaster Areas: The National Government Flood Relief Commission allocated a large amount of relief wheat to the disaster-stricken areas east of Jiangbei. A reporting station was set up in Tianshenggang, Nantong, for transshipment. More than 6,000 tons have already been transported, and a second batch of 7,000 tons is expected to arrive from Shanghai within days.

Police Inspectorates in Various Counties of Jiangbei to be Abolished: Each of the counties of Tong, Ru, Hai, and Tai in Jiangbei has established 25 military inspectorates. Shang Xihe, the chief inspector of the Nantong General Inspectorate, had a conflict with Supervisor Zhang Xinyu last year. Zhang was arrested and released two days later. Zhang went to the province to file a complaint. The provincial commander-in-chief has ordered the abolition of all county inspectorates. It is heard that this will be implemented soon, and Shang Xihe has already left Tong.

Changzhou

Accidental Shooting Causes Death: Jin Quansheng, a villager from Shengan Village, Tianjing Township, Wuyi Sixth District, was hunting animals with a shotgun near the Land Temple at about 1:00 PM on the 6th when, due to carelessness, he accidentally shot and killed Zhang Genbao, the son of Zhang Chen. The district office reported the case to the County Court. Chief Prosecutor Yang Kongyi led officials to conduct an examination on the 7th.

Nanjing

Results of the National Electrical Engineering Technical Committee Election Announced: During the annual meeting of the National Electrical Engineering Association held in Nanjing last year, the Technical Committee also held a concurrent conference. Xu Dongren was elected as the chairman, Shen Sifang was elected as the vice-chairman, and Zhang Baigang, Zhang Shitong, Zhi Bingyuan, Deng Zian, and Sun Shihua were elected as standing committee members. Huzhou

Notes on Robbery Cases: In Dongjia Village near Shuikou Town in the western suburbs of this city, a farmer named Chen Qing has abundant property, attracting the covetous eyes of bandits. At around 10:00 PM on the 30th of last month, more than ten bandits, each carrying a pistol and flashlight, broke down the door and entered. Hearing the noise, Aqing escaped through the back door. Seeing that Chen had fled, the bandits kidnapped his newlywed wife. Also, in Tushan, near Shuanglin, there is a Land Temple. The abbot, Asi, has been managing the temple for many years. Suddenly, at around 11:00 PM the day before yesterday, seven or eight bandits, each carrying knives and clubs, broke into the temple and tied up Asi, demanding money. Asi was seriously injured, and all his clothing and bedding were robbed, totaling a loss of more than fifty yuan.

Arrived at the Department at 10:00 AM to Take Over

Summoned All Staff for a Speech

Director Chen of the Zhejiang Education Department arrived at the department at around 10:00 AM on the 7th to take over his duties. He announced that Lin Duan would be transferred to Secretary, He Jingyu would be Superintendent and Acting Secretary, Lu Dianyang would be the head of the First Section, Zhang Rentian would be the head of the Third Section, and Li Zhenxia would be the head of the Fourth Section. This time, he was ordered to return to Zhejiang to manage education. Due to the recurrence of his old heart condition recently, he repeatedly requested to resign, but his request was not granted, so he had to temporarily take on the responsibility. Director Zhang had spared no effort in planning and reorganizing education in the province over the past year. His loyalty and responsible spirit are admired by the entire province. The achievements of the Education Department in the past year are a great improvement compared to when he himself was in Zhejiang. This is due to the appropriate guidance of Director Zhang, as well as the joint efforts of all colleagues. At a time when the national crisis is deepening, saving the nation and wiping out humiliation, education is particularly important. He sincerely hopes that all colleagues will continue to work hard and assist him so as not to fail. This is the fortune of education in the province. All plans will be implemented as originally scheduled and can still be discussed at any time. It is heard that the department secretary, Qian Jia, and section chief, Luo Di, will continue to hold their positions, and superintendents such as Feng Keshu will also remain in their positions without much change. Although he has made an effort to arrive at the department despite his illness, he still needs to rest from time to time.

Vice Minister Qian of the Ministry of Education Submits His Resignation Again

Qian Changzhao, the Permanent Vice Minister of the Ministry of Education, submitted a request to the Executive Yuan to resign after the closing of the plenary session of the Central Committee, but it has not been approved. Because Minister Li resigned and left the ministry, and Political Vice Minister Chen Bulei went to Zhejiang to take up his new position, and Minister Zhu has not yet taken over his duties, no one is in charge of the ministry, so he continues to go to the ministry to work as usual. Vice Minister Qian believes that someone is responsible for the ministry's affairs and has submitted another request to the Executive Yuan to resign from his current position so that he can be relieved of his responsibilities as soon as possible.

Measures for Internships of Anhui Students Studying Abroad

Have Been Revised and Filed with the Ministry of Education

The Anhui Education Department previously received an order from the Ministry of Education, ordering it to draft regulations for internships for graduates of colleges and universities in Europe and the United States majoring in that province and submit them for review and approval. Based on this, it revised the previous regulations for internships for Anhui students in Europe and the United States, adding improvements where necessary. The content is divided into six articles, named "Revised Measures for Internships for Anhui Provincial-Funded Students and Scholarship Students Studying Abroad," and submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval. Recently, it has been instructed to be approved and filed. The revised internship measures are appended below:

(1) If the major of a provincial-funded student or scholarship student requires an internship after graduation, they should first state the reason and submit a plan for approval by the Education Department, which will then send a letter to the embassy or study abroad supervisor in the country where they are located to introduce them to a well-known venue for an internship. (2) If there are special circumstances regarding the internship location of a provincial-funded student or scholarship student, and an introduction from the school is required, the school should provide a letter of proof that has been approved by the department before the internship can be conducted. (3) Internships for provincial-funded students and scholarship students are limited to the four fields of science, engineering, agriculture, and medicine. The internship period is set at one year. If necessary, it can be extended by six months or one year after approval. (4) Provincial-funded students and scholarship students will continue to receive their original fees during the internship. (5) After the internship of a provincial-funded student or scholarship student has been approved, they must submit the date of commencement of the internship, along with a certificate of internship, to the department for verification. They must also fill out and submit a report on the status and experience of the internship every three months in accordance with the academic report form for filing. (6) If a provincial-funded student or scholarship student violates the provisions of these measures, the payment of fees will be stopped.

Petitioning Students of Anhui University Return to School

They were received by Zhu Wenzhong, the secretary of the National Government.
