The representatives believed that their responsibility for petitioning had ended and immediately took a boat back to school to report.

A Tea Party Will Be Held at the YMCA at 4:00 PM Today

To Discuss All Matters Related to the Conclusion of the Preparatory Committee

The Preparatory Committee of the Shanghai University Faculty and Staff Association is scheduled to hold a tea party in the Western Restaurant on the 9th floor of the YMCA in Baixianqiao at 4:00 PM today (the 8th) to conclude all preparatory matters and discuss the date, method, and procedure for convening the Representative Assembly. There will be important proposals at that time. It is also heard that representatives from various well-known national and private universities in Shanghai have been produced one after another, and the registration has been very enthusiastic in recent days. However, the person in charge of the association solemnly declared to the outside world that the association is a purely free and moral combination with no compulsory nature. Non-branch members of the Chinese should respect the personality and will of others and not be jealous or slanderous. The total number of members of the association has now reached more than 865.

The Anti-Japanese United Association of Middle School Students Held Its 15th Representative Congress Yesterday

Discussing the Funding Proposal for the Petitioning Delegation

The 16th Meeting Will Continue Today

The Delegation to Petition in Beijing Issues an Important Declaration

The Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association of Middle School Students in this city held its 15th Representative Congress at Jingye Middle School in Jukui Street, Xiaodongmen, at 10:00 AM yesterday (the 7th). Attendees included more than 40 representatives from 29 schools including Shanghai Jiang, Huiling, and Shanghai Middle School. The presidium included Xie Jinbiao from Shanghai Jiang, Kang Dingxia from Shanghai Middle School, and Ding Dezhao from Huiling. The recorder was Fan Xifan from Shanghai Middle School. (1) Reporting Items: (A) The Inspection Team Reported on the Reorganization Process; (B) The Representatives of the Delegation to Petition in Beijing Reported on the Opening Process; (C) The Presidium Reported on the Request to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to Strike. (2) Matters for Discussion: (A) The proposal to carry the remaining 108 yuan and 67 cents from the previous delegation to petition in Beijing as the funding for this delegation was approved. (B) The proposal to request a subsidy for the delegation to petition in Beijing was approved to subsidize 200 yuan. (C) The proposal from the Daxia representatives that the purpose of the previous petition to Beijing was too vague and should be corrected was decided to be submitted to the delegation meeting for discussion. It is also heard that the association is scheduled to continue its 16th Representative Congress at Jingye at 10:00 AM this morning to discuss urgent matters. It is hoped that representatives from various schools will attend at that time. It is also heard that the association's delegation to petition in Beijing went to Beijing at 11:30 PM last night and issued an important official statement as follows: Dear compatriots, in this time of wind and rain and increasing national danger, a sudden thunderclap revealed that Jinzhou, a key gateway for our two northeastern provinces, has been captured by the invading army. The bad news has broken our hearts. From now on, hundreds of thousands of square miles of beautiful rivers and mountains outside Shanhaiguan will never be ours, and millions of people will have to lower their heads and submit to the tyranny of foreign races and the taste of being slaves to a lost nation. Seeing the fragmentation of the rivers and mountains and lamenting the daily failures of national affairs, how can we, the youth who possess both reason and passion, sit back and watch the mountains and rivers of our motherland be plunged into foreign lands without concern? Therefore, this time we are holding the supreme determination and unprecedented courage to represent the hundreds of thousands of middle school students in Shanghai in this third trip to Beijing. On the one hand, we will urge the government, which intends to muddle through internally and is helpless and numb to the outside world, to immediately send troops to recover the lost land. On the other hand, we will plan for the nation's rise and fall, which is the responsibility of every man, and ask our hundreds of thousands of middle school classmates to take on the task of punishing Japan. Since we bear such a major mission this time, we can only uphold our spirit of courage and directness and make the most effort to fight on behalf of the hundreds of thousands of middle school students. We will not care about any sacrifices. After accepting the order, we respectfully declare the above.

Talents Hired by the Vocational Guidance Institute

The Vocational Guidance Institute at No. 80 Hualong Road, Shanghai, has recently been entrusted by a certain school in Pudong to hire a kindergarten teacher and an art female teacher, both of whom must have considerable experience with a monthly salary of about 25 yuan, including food and lodging. A certain middle school in Fujian has entrusted them to hire a female teacher who must be a graduate of a professional school or above, preferably with a degree in education or medicine, to teach English, social studies, education, natural science, and mathematics, and must also teach singing, dancing, home economics, and women's work, teaching 15 hours per week, with a monthly salary of 60 to 70 yuan. Another male teacher is required to be a graduate of a professional school and have rich experience or have worked as a factory technician for many years, to teach civil engineering (with the ability to make various new types of wooden utensils), bamboo work, rattan work, papermaking, and also serve as the director of the vocational department, with a monthly salary of 60 to 80 yuan. A certain agency in Nanjing has entrusted them to hire an accountant who must be a graduate of a university with a degree in commerce and have more than three years of accounting experience to be qualified, with a monthly salary of 80 yuan. A certain weaving factory in Guangzhou has entrusted them to hire an iron machine weaving instructor who must have experience in managing weaving machinery, with a monthly salary of 30 yuan. A certain publishing house has entrusted them to hire an editor who must be old and have editing experience to be qualified, with a monthly salary to be negotiated (applicants must bring publications and works they have edited). A certain seed farm in this province has entrusted them to recruit a number of salespersons who are familiar with the farmers of Wujiang, Zhenze, Wuxi, and Jiangyin to be qualified, regardless of gender, with generous commissions. A certain middle school in Changzhou has entrusted them to hire an electrical and mechanical teacher and an analytical geometry and integral calculus teacher, each with a monthly salary of about 70 yuan. Also, the institute is recruiting several students from Shanghai Shishi Vocational Night School to test for work, with full-length tuition and discretionary subsidies. The exam will be held at the institute at 9:00 AM this Saturday. Any male or female student who has graduated from junior high school and is interested in learning Chinese typing, clerical work, bookkeeping, etc. can register at the institute immediately.

Overcoming Perseverance and Striving for the YMCA Championship

| Perseverance Lost in the Last Three Minutes |

The Result Was 44 to 38

YMCA overcame their strong opponent Perseverance in an unpredictable state last night in the last three minutes. Although they had suffered a setback before, they still had hope for the Western Youth Basketball Championship. In Group B, YMCA Middle School defeated Evening Star 27-24.

Cheng Jingxing Settles the World

In the unpredictable ball battle, when there were three minutes left, Gu Guangdao scored a goal from afar, and Perseverance took the lead by one point, with its momentum gaining, and it seemed that victory was at hand. However, he repeatedly threw from afar, seeking victory too much, and only saw that he wasted the opportunity in vain. Cheng Jingxing of Cheng Jingxing, holding a halberd and riding a horse, waited for an opportunity and held a ball in his hand, which was successful. YMCA was more than one point ahead, and the military spirit was greatly enhanced. Chen Xianglong and Wu Youliang worked together, scoring three goals in a row, and the victory was decided. Lin Zequn's penalty of one point was like icing on the cake.

Yang Linyu Takes the Lead by One Goal

In the sound of the start of the battle, Gu Guangdao stood out from the camp and opened the record for Perseverance. Yang Linyu reversed and scored a basket, leading YMCA by four to zero. Cheng Jing three arrows in the middle, Hou and Chen also helped each other, leading by ten to four in turn. Yang's two goals and Guangdao's one goal became equal again. Both sides were relaxed and focused on strategies. The differences between them depended on the fate of the throw. YMCA once led by nineteen to twelve, but before the halftime whistle, one goal by Yang Linyu allowed Perseverance to lead the first half by twenty-two to twenty-one.

Perseverance Failed Due to Long Shots

In the second half, Perseverance took the lead step by step, and YMCA chased closely step by step. Although the difference was small, the momentum of Perseverance's ball was smoother. Unfortunately, they wasted too much on long shots, and failure lies in this point. At that time, Perseverance once led YMCA by thirty to twenty-four, and YMCA also led by thirty-seven to thirty-four. The changes in this are countless. Until the last three minutes, they were attacked by YMCA, resulting in a failure of thirty-eight to forty-four. The referees were Shu Ming and Shao Ji.

City First Industrial & Commercial Football Tournament to Begin

69 Teams to Compete Starting on the 9th

Field Rentals Suspended on Saturdays and Sundays

The City First Public Stadium Fourth Industrial and Commercial Amateur Football Competition Committee held a meeting yesterday to review the teams and arrange the groups. A total of 69 teams were approved to join the competition, divided into six groups according to their level: People, Fitness, and National Salvation. The People group has the most teams, so it is divided into three subgroups: Industry, Commerce. Round-robin matches will be held. The Fitness group and the Strong group are next, divided into two subgroups: Industry and Commerce. The remaining groups have fewer teams and are not divided into subgroups. Therefore, the People, Fitness, and Strong groups will have champions and runners-up, while the Fitness, National Salvation groups will only have champions and no runners-up. The competition dates are Saturdays afternoons and Sundays all day, to avoid interfering with business. It is expected to last from January 9th to May 8th. Therefore, during these four months, all school and group rentals for practice or meetings on Saturday afternoons and Sundays will not be allowed, as there is only one football field. If further delayed, the weather will become too hot to complete the competition.

Local News

New Mayor Wu Tiecheng Took Office Yesterday

Central Government and National Government Sent Personnel to Supervise the Oath

Announced the Appointments of Bureau Chiefs and Section Chiefs

The newly appointed Mayor of this city, Mr. Wu Tiecheng, held an oath-taking ceremony at the City Government in Fenglin Bridge at 10:00 AM yesterday. Chen Bijun, sent by the Central Party Headquarters to supervise the oath, was unable to attend due to illness. Kong Xiangxi, representative of the National Government, and Chen Qun, representative of the Executive Yuan, both attended the ceremony to supervise the oath. Former Mayor Zhang also gave a speech. More than a thousand guests attended. The details of each item are recorded separately below:

Solemn Venue The city government gate hung the Party and national flags. In the auditorium hung the portrait of the late Dr. Sun Yat-sen. The city government road was lined with police officers from the City Public Security Bureau, stationed with strict sentries. An armed patrol team of the police brigade guarded in front of the gate. The police maintained order inside the venue, and city government staff served as greeters. The military band of the Public Security Bureau played music.

Wu Tiecheng Takes the Oath The new Mayor Wu Tiecheng raised his right hand and swore, "I solemnly swear that I will abide by the will of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen, obey the Party's principles, abide by the laws, be loyal and diligent in my duties. I will never waste a penny, misuse a person, nor engage in corruption or bribery. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the most severe punishment." This oath.

Kong Xiangxi's Speech Central oath supervisor Kong Xiangxi said briefly that Shanghai is not only China's leading commercial port but also a world-class metropolis. At this time when the country is in trouble and the national crisis is heavy, the person in charge must not only bear the heavy responsibility of local affairs but also cope with major diplomatic tasks. Among the past mayors, Mayor Zhang Yuejun has served the longest. He and his colleagues in the city government have had concrete plans for the development of industry and commerce and the progress of construction. Now there is also the construction of the city center area. Mayor Zhang has worked hard for several years, so he intends to rest temporarily and sincerely resigned to the central government. The central government then sent Mr. Wu Tiecheng to lead Shanghai. Mr. Wu has followed the late Premier Sun Yat-sen for a long time and has a deep history with the Party. He has rich experience and knowledge. His appointment as Mayor of this city is not only a blessing for the citizens but also for the Party and the country. However, the development of this city still depends on the citizens, so the cooperation between the citizens and Mayor Wu is necessary for Shanghai to be successful. The late Premier Sun Yat-sen worked hard for the revolution, and his only goal was to realize the Three Principles of the People. The most important of the Three Principles of the People is to realize democratic politics, with the people exercising political power. When the task of governance is completed in the future, it will be time for popular elections. But this matter must start with local autonomy. I hope that Shanghai will start from local autonomy and complete local autonomy. The responsibility lies with the Mayor, but it must be helped by all the citizens of Shanghai to succeed.

Chen Renhe's Speech Executive Yuan oath supervisor Chen Qun (Renhe) said briefly that when Mayor Wu was the head of Xiangshan County, Guangdong, he was not appointed by the governor of the province but was personally appointed by the President. This proves that the President personally handed over the task to the head of Xiangshan County. Now that he is Mayor, he will surely work hard. There are now some bureaucrats who often do things perfunctorily, and the people of the country cannot benefit. Mayor Wu will surely do things based on the people's standpoint. I hope Mayor Wu will not cooperate with a few celebrities representing Shanghai but with the truly full city.

Tong Xingbai's Speech

City Party representative Tong Xingbai said briefly that Mayor Wu has a close relationship with the Party, so after he takes office as Mayor of Shanghai, he will surely make the Party and government work more closely. The two most important cases resolved by the Shanghai Sixth and Seventh Representative Congresses are: (1) The construction of the city center area. The former Mayor has spent many days of effort on this and has worked hard to manage it. This cannot be completed in two or three years and requires ten or twenty years of effort to be effective. Its relationship not only leads to the development of industry and commerce but also affects politics and diplomacy. Therefore, I hope that Mayor Wu will complete it as soon as possible to comfort the people of Shanghai. (2) On the issue of local autonomy, democratic politics is based on local autonomy. Therefore, there must be a broad mass of workers, peasants, merchants, and civilians engaged in local autonomy to achieve true democratic politics. Now I only hear people talk about democratic politics and do not hear people talk about local autonomy. It is really talking about the branches and neglecting the root. Therefore, I hope that Mayor Wu will work hard on local autonomy so that it can be completed as soon as possible, so that the citizens can participate in the opportunity of popular elections.

Zhang Yuejun's Speech

Today is the day that Mayor Wu takes office, and it is also the day that I relinquish my responsibility. Everyone must be clear about Mayor Wu's knowledge, talent, and contributions to the Party and the country, without waiting for me to praise him. Today, I am honored to participate in the grand ceremony of his inauguration. Based on my feelings, there are about three points. The first point is to contribute to Mayor Wu. The ancients said that the policies of the old magistrate should be told to the new magistrate. This word "tell" is very meaningful. On the surface, it seems reasonable, but in fact, it is the most sincere expression of responsibility for each other. I am not talented, and I am willing to fulfill the obligation of the word "tell" by contributing my opinions. I have been in office since April of the 18th year until today, when I hand over the responsibilities, for a term of two years and more than nine months. During this term, I believe that the most noteworthy things are three things. The first is the construction of Greater Shanghai. This is the expectation of the general public, and it is also the common mentality of the central government, the national people, and even the people of China and foreign countries. Since I took office, I have spared no effort to devote all my energy to achieve this goal as soon as possible. However, to achieve this goal, we must base it on the construction of the city center area. Regarding this planning and everything that has happened, I have issued a special publication to explain it during the groundbreaking ceremony of the new city government building in the city center area last year. Now the new city government building will be completed by the end of this year. After it is completed, it can be moved. On the one hand, a custodian committee has been set up to manage the fund for the city center. This is the foundation that has been laid, and it is not difficult to progress step by step to complete the construction of Greater Shanghai. This is one. The second is the stability of Shanghai. Shanghai is the cultural center of the country and the hub of transportation between China and foreign countries. Its importance is beyond words. At this time of internal and external troubles, if we can maintain the order of Shanghai and prevent it from being disrupted, and ensure the stability of Shanghai and prevent it from being shaken, it will surely have a very good impact on the country both internally and externally. On the contrary, its impact can also be asserted. Since I took office, I have been thinking about this day and night, neglecting sleep and forgetting food, and not hesitating to complain, so that I can quickly respond to the internal and external opportunities for more than 100 days. And every Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday, I gather with the authorities and people from all walks of life to discuss and negotiate ways to deal with it. This is also the reason. This is two. The third is the spirit of cooperation between the Shanghai Municipal Government and the citizens. From the standpoint of the Mayor, on the one hand, he is a member of the central government, and on the other hand, he is a servant of the citizens. On the other hand, he must also work together with the local Party and government organs to fulfill his duties. However, the central government and the local Party and government organs are all on the government side, and the citizens are the masters of the Mayor. Therefore, there must be close cooperation between the master and the servant to avoid regrets. Since I took office, I have sought to accommodate the opinions of local people from all walks of life as much as possible for all matters concerning the implementation of city government and the reform of various matters, and to give them the opportunity to participate in planning, in order to harmonize and avoid estrangement. Therefore, in the past two or three years, I have received the guidance of the citizens of the whole city, which has benefited me greatly. These three things are sincerely contributed to Mayor Wu for reference. I am ashamed of my short talent and lack of adequate performance. There are many things that need to be carried out by Mayor Wu's efforts. Mayor Wu's talent is a hundred times greater than mine, and he cannot develop his grand plans to benefit the citizens of this city. The second point is to encourage the Shanghai Municipal Government and the colleagues of the various bureaus under its jurisdiction. Since the establishment of the Shanghai Municipal Government, it will be five years. Since the founding of the first Mayor Huang, all personnel administration has had a certain standard. I, Zhang, the former Mayor, succeeded and served as the leader of Shanghai for more than two years. I have done my best to follow the old model for various administrative matters, and most of the personnel still retain their old positions. Today, Shanghai's municipal administration has this kind of achievement, which has not been the result of the joint efforts of all the colleagues of the municipal government and various bureaus. We all serve the country and the people, and we should all follow the spirit of consistency from beginning to end, and strive hard from top to bottom. Although I am now leaving office, the spirit of mutual struggle in the past two or three years will always be unforgettable. I deeply hope that the Shanghai Municipal Government and the colleagues of the various bureaus under its jurisdiction will work together to support Mayor Wu with what they used to support me, so that the success of this city will be unlimited, the future of all colleagues will be unlimited, and Mayor Wu's knowledge and experience are very rich, and all colleagues will benefit infinitely from his leadership. Today, when I am about to leave, I would like to briefly contribute a few words as an example of the ancient people's gifts, hoping that all colleagues will work harder. The third point is to hope that the people from all walks of life in this city will be the Mayor, who should be elected by the people. The period of political tutelage is therefore a transitional measure taken by the Central Committee. However, on the one hand, it is appointed by the Central Committee, and on the other hand, it cannot be prepared for the people's election. Therefore, all municipal facilities should be cooperated by the government and the people to gradually advance to the course of the people's election. Moreover, the period from political tutelage to constitutional government is not far away and will arrive in the blink of an eye. During this shortest period, I deeply hope that the people and people from all walks of life in this city will fully prepare their work. The so-called preparatory work is to work closely with the Municipal Government. The three things that I contributed to Mayor Wu in the first point, such as the construction of Greater Shanghai, the stability of Shanghai, and the spirit of cooperation between the Shanghai Municipal Government and the citizens, cannot be achieved by the efforts of the government alone, and they cannot be achieved by the efforts of one hand and one foot. During my tenure, I have received the guidance of people from all walks of life, and the trust and support of the citizens of the whole city. Therefore, I can express the spirit of cooperation as much as possible and there is no estrangement, so that all facilities of the Municipal Government can be promoted. This time, I resigned, and I was also begged by people from all walks of life to stay. My feelings are sincere and I cannot say. However, our common goal is to complete the construction of Greater Shanghai, maintain the stability of Shanghai, and the spirit of cooperation between the government and the citizens. I deeply believe that Mayor Wu will be able to achieve this goal, so I also hope that people from all walks of life and the citizens of the whole city will trust Mayor Wu with the trust that I have from you and trust that Mayor Wu will cooperate with sincerity and there will be no limit to the bright future. Today, Mayor Wu is the Mayor appointed by the Central Committee. In the future, he may be the Mayor elected by you. If you want to achieve the goal of the Mayor's election by the people, you must strive to express the spirit of cooperation. I will pay my respects to you at the time of my departure, and I wish you infinite hope.

Mayor Wu's Reply

Shanghai is the center of national finance and industry and commerce, and also the hub of culture and transportation. In terms of this country, it is the largest commercial port in the country. In terms of the world, it also occupies an important position. Premier Sun Yat-sen paid great attention to the development of major ports in the East and the construction of Greater Shanghai in the Outline of National Construction. The Municipal Government has been established for five years. Through the planning of previous mayors, especially Mayor Zhang's efforts in the construction of the city center area during his more than two years in office, the planning is meticulous, well-organized, and has achieved remarkable results. With this excellent scale, I will continue to actively promote it in the future to ensure that those who have already been handled will be completed as soon as possible and those who have not yet started will be gradually organized, so that the construction plan will be promoted to realization one by one. The three points that Mayor Zhang encouraged, and the realization of local autonomy proposed by Comrade Tong, the representative of the City Party, I will sincerely accept. The essence of the new city organization law is also in the realization of local autonomy. I have long regarded it as one of the important goals of governance and will definitely strive to achieve it. I would like to earnestly and sincerely tell the leaders of the circles and the citizens of the whole city that this time I have taken office as the Mayor of Shanghai, not to be an official, but to serve the people with a spirit of sacrifice, and to build a new Shanghai City with order, rules, prosperity, and perfection, so that Shanghai can be lived and worked in peace and contentment by the citizens of the whole city, and the industry and commerce can gradually develop. However, it must be achieved through the guidance of various circles, the support of the citizens of the whole city, and the concerted efforts of the Municipal Government and the colleagues of all subordinate organs. This city has the most developed industry and commerce in the country, so labor-capital disputes are inevitable. I believe that this kind of dispute is an unavoidable stage in the progress of modern society, but if it can be reconciled fairly, it is not difficult to resolve it. However, China's economy is backward, and industrialists and merchants are still immature, and we should do our best to maintain and develop it. Moreover, China does not have big capitalists. It only relies on small property owners to make industrial and commercial attempts. If disputes arise from time to time, the impact will be very great, so we should devote ourselves to labor-capital cooperation and guide them in detail to make them friendly to each other. Then there will be hope for the development of various industries in the future. After the realization of the construction of the city center area, the administrative industry and commerce will be concentrated in one area, and the administrative orders and facilities will increase efficiency, and the industrial and commercial industries will observe each other and compete in a regulated manner. Its development and progress will be even more impressive. I will never easily change the subordinates of the Municipal Government if they work hard and achieve great results. The above statements are just a few points. In addition, such as how to reorganize the land and the urgent need to popularize education, all of which are the responsibilities that the Municipal Government should bear. I will do my best with my colleagues to create a new Shanghai with order, regulation, prosperity, and tranquility. I hope that the leaders of various circles and the citizens of the whole city will supervise and educate me from time to time, and submit written statements on the reform and development of municipal administration. I will sincerely accept it. It is a great honor to make up for the shortcomings.

Newly Appointed Officials

After Mayor Wu took office, all section chiefs, secretaries, and bureau chiefs who had resigned and were approved were immediately reappointed. The list of their names is recorded below: Secretary and Chief of the First Section Sun Pu, Chief of the Third Section Zhu Fengfu, Secretary Zhang Zhenxi, Assistant Secretary Huang Jianfen, Counselor Sun Sheng, Director of the Public Security Bureau Wen Yingxing, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau Mai Chaochu, Director of the Land Bureau Jin Liren, Deputy Director of the Business Tax Collection Office Zhou Xin. As for the former Counselor and Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, he has been formally appointed by Mayor Wu as the Secretary-General of the Municipal Government.

Zhang Qun Presents to the National Government

After former Mayor Zhang Qun resigned, he reported to the National Government Executive Yuan: "The National Government Executive Yuan of Nanjing is informed that I have requested to resign, and I have been ordered to approve it, and Wu Tiecheng has been appointed as the Mayor of Shanghai. I will relinquish my duties on the Guangri day and have handed over everything clearly. In addition to telexing the National Government Executive, I would like to report by telegram and ask for your review. Zhang Qun bows and submits."

Proclamation of Taking Office

For the sake of proclamation, on January 6th of this year, I received the No. 25 Appointment Letter from the National Government, appointing Wu Tiecheng as the Mayor of Xiaoshanghai. Based on this letter, etc., I, the Mayor, took the oath on January 7th and took charge of the seal and took office. In addition to reporting and separately sending letters, I hereby issue a proclamation for general knowledge. This proclamation.

Wang Jingwei Resigns from Both Standing Committee Positions by Telegram

Wang Jingwei sent a telegram to the Central Committee in Nanjing, saying, "The Political Conference of the Central Committee of the Nanjing Party is informed that I was previously elected as a Standing Committee member. I know that my talent is not enough to win, and I only think that when the country is in trouble, it is enough to get a little better, so I can take the road with all my strength, so I dare not resign. However, I have been serving for more than ten days, and there is no improvement. I have been stealing the name for a long time, and I feel guilty. After thinking again and again, I can only apply to be relieved of the positions of Standing Committee Member of the Central Committee and Standing Committee Member of the Political Conference, so as not to hinder office work. I hope you will agree. Wang Zhaoming Yang."

Business Circles Send Urgent Telegrams Against Japan

City Chamber of Commerce Asks for Quick Decision on Major Plans The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the National Government yesterday, saying, "The National Government of Nanjing is informed that the Japanese army has occupied Jinzhou and is approaching Shanhaiguan and invading Rehe. The outrageous riots have become more and more. At this time when the political situation is newly established and the whole country is looking forward to it, we earnestly hope that you will quickly decide on major plans, rectify the army, use force to recover the lost land, implement revolutionary diplomacy, act on your words, and act quickly. All the merchants and people of Shanghai are waiting for orders. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce bows and submits."

City Federation of Commerce Solemnly Expresses The Shanghai Municipal Federation of People and the Shanghai General Federation of Business Circles jointly telegraphed the National Government and the Executive Yuan yesterday on the Sino-Japanese diplomatic compromise, specifically representing all the merchants and people of Shanghai, solemnly expressing: "Chairman Lin of the National Government of Nanjing and Dean Sun of the Executive Yuan are informed that the Western newspapers in Shanghai reported that Foreign Minister Chen has been secretly negotiating with the representatives of the Japanese, and there is also a proposal to promote ambassadors to each other. I think that the Japanese have violated the agreement to withdraw troops, and even occupied Jinzhou, and threatened Shanhaiguan, and even coveted Pingjin and Qingji. Under this situation, our country adheres to Premier Sun Yat-sen's teachings and seeks an independent, free, and equal country. How should we rectify the military and act quickly to mobilize and drive the Japanese troops out of our territory and make them surrender and seek peace? However, news came that they were secretly compromising, which is tantamount to an alliance under the city, and it goes without saying that it is a negotiation that loses national sovereignty. The outspoken remarks of Bao Mingqian at the Xinghualou Restaurant in Shanghai at the banquet of the Pacific Society caused a great uproar, but he was appointed as the Director of the European and American Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. In this way, the compromise with the Japanese is even more traceable. Therefore, we specifically solemnly express that all the results of the negotiations with the Japanese by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs that lose national sovereignty will not be recognized by all the merchants and people of Shanghai. We respectfully ask Minister Chen to pay attention. We are extremely fearful of this urgent telegram. The Shanghai Municipal Federation of People and the Shanghai General Federation of Business Circles bow and submit together."

Telegraph to Avoid Sino-Japanese Plans

The National Salvation Association of the Republic of China telegraphed: "The National Government of Nanjing and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs are informed that the Japanese have captured Jinzhou and are driving deep into the country. We have heard that their secret plan is to first intimidate them, then adopt a means of wanting to catch and letting go, and entice our government to sign a contract to hand over the rights of way and all economic rights and interests. Finally, they will use a large loan to bait us and manipulate our national government. There is even a secret plan that has already been carried out and that we have tacitly agreed to. The Association has heard about it in secret and cannot but ask. If there is no such thing, please announce it clearly and use all our strength to recover the lost land. If we fall into their tricks, the people will never recognize it. The National Salvation Association of the Republic of China bows and submits, Yu."

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Sailors Demand Salaries, Leading to a Shipping Strike

All Twelve Ships in Shanghai Stop Sailing

Ningbo and Yangtze River Ships Not Operating

All sailors of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, demanding equal treatment with the company employees and requesting the issuance of double year-end salaries, were rejected by Guo Waifeng. Yesterday, due to the failure of the petition, all sailors stopped working. The commercial ships in Shanghai have all stopped sailing, and traffic on the rivers and seas is completely blocked, the situation is very serious. The reporter conducted a thorough investigation of the before and after of this matter, and the details are recorded as follows:

Request for Double Salaries: At the end of December last year, when the company employees were paid double salaries, all sailors, seamen, stokers, etc., also sent an official letter to Guo Waifeng, requesting that the sailors' treatment be the same as that of the company employees and that double salaries also be given. Subsequently, Guo Waifeng replied and rejected the request, saying that the sailors' treatment was better than that of the company employees, so the request was difficult to approve. The sailors and seamen then asked Mr. Li Zhengwu to mediate and consult with Guo, but were also strictly rejected by Guo Waifeng. This matter had no result. Yesterday, the ships that had sailed out returned to Shanghai one after another, and the sailors decided to go to the company together to meet with Guo and request supplementary payments, determined to achieve their goal.

Meeting with the General Manager: Yesterday morning at 9:00, the sailors from twelve ships, including Xin Jiangtian, Jiangtian, Jiang'an, Jianghua, Haiyan, Guangli, Guangji, Xinming, Gongping, Emei, Taishun, and Tonghua, a total of thirty or forty people, went to the company to meet with Guo Waifeng and request the issuance of double salaries. Guo had not yet arrived at the company when the sailors arrived. Li Yuncheng, the head of the shipping department, met with them on his behalf. Li ordered each ship to send a representative. Shortly after Guo arrived at the company, twelve sailor representatives met with Guo, stating that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company was an institution directly under the National Government and that the treatment of its employees should be the same as that of the customs, railways, and post offices, with supplementary issuance of double salaries to show fairness. Guo told the representatives that the sailors' treatment was better than that of the company employees. The year-end double salary for the company employees was a special arrangement by the commissioner to adjust the economic situation of each person. It was difficult to issue double salaries to the sailors. If the sailors could cancel this request, they could help each other to overcome the difficult situation. If they insisted on demanding double salaries, he would have to resign and leave. There was no result, and they dispersed.

Group Meetings: The representatives returned to their ships and reported this to the stokers, seamen, etc., expressing their despair. From 1:00 PM, the sailors from each ship went to the steering, engine, river pilot, and other associations, while the sailors went to the Jun'an Association, etc., to convene group meetings to discuss the issue of demanding double salaries and the unpaid wages for December. The results of the various meetings were unanimously decided to take further measures. The All Sailors Petition Group of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company was established, representative committee members were elected, and a declaration was drafted to seek social assistance.

All Ships Stop Sailing: After the establishment of the Petition Group, all employees decided that, starting from today (the 7th), the twelve ships that had arrived in Shanghai, including Xin Jiangtian, Jiangtian, Jiang'an, Jianghua, Haiyan, Guangji, Guangli, Taishun, Xinming, Emei, Gongping, and Tonghua, would all stop sailing. The employees on the ships also stopped working from yesterday afternoon. The ships were all anchored at the Jinliyuan Wharf. If the double salary issue is not resolved, the ships will not sail. The ships that are scheduled to arrive tomorrow and the day after tomorrow will also be asked to join the strike.

Traffic Blocked: Yesterday, the ships that were scheduled to depart included the Ningbo ship Xin Jiangtian, the Yangtze River ships Jiang'an and Jianghua, the Fuzhou ship Guangli, the Wenzhou ship Guangji, and the Nanhua ship Taishun, all loading goods and passengers at the South Wharf. The passengers on the Xin Jiangtian were even more crowded. After the sailors decided to stop sailing in the afternoon, the Xin Jiangtian temporarily refunded tickets, and passengers changed to the Sanbei Ningxing ship. The goods that had been loaded onto the ship were also unloaded and reloaded onto other ships. The export goods of the other four ships were also temporarily stopped from loading, and passengers scrambled to refund tickets because there was no hope of departure. The wharf was very tense for a while, and river and sea traffic was greatly disrupted.

Petition Declaration: Since the reorganization of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, the company employees have been given double salaries at the end of each year, but not the sailors. The sailors feel that the treatment is unfair, so they have repeatedly made verbal requests to the authorities, but Commissioner Zhao has shown no sincerity, delaying and undermining the requests, so they have not been successful. Commissioner Guo took over and followed the same pattern. The colleagues were negotiating with Li when Li suddenly left his post. At the time of his departure, he gave the company employees a bonus of one and a half months' salary and a bonus of about 40% of each person's salary. The sailors were in an uproar, but Li had already left his post, and the successor ignored it, so it became an unresolved issue. Because the colleagues had been repeatedly deceived by the authorities, they sent a letter to Guo Ren in November of last year, requesting equal treatment with the company employees and the issuance of double salaries based on the principles of the Kuomintang to improve the lives and safeguard the interests of workers and technicians. However, Commissioner Guo evaded the issue, and because the colleagues had no verbal evidence, they asked him to reply in writing. He agreed to reply by phone, but the date was postponed from today to tomorrow. It was not until December 28 of last year that a letter was received, but the content was completely inconsistent with the facts, and the words were sophistical. While claiming that the company was in economic difficulty, he issued double salaries to the company employees (on the 28th). The colleagues refuted it item by item, and Mr. Huanwu mediated, but Commissioner Guo still evaded the issue and postponed it from today to tomorrow, giving only lip service. The colleagues believe that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is a state-owned institution, and all employees are public servants. All duties are just each person's division of labor and cooperation, so there should be no difference in treatment. Moreover, the sailors are profit-making, and the company employees are profit-sharing, but the reward of double salaries is the opposite, which is really too unfair. Therefore, they had no choice but to go to the company together today (the 7th) to petition for the issuance of double salaries. Commissioner Guo received them, and the colleagues fully expected that he would give a satisfactory reply, but the commissioner evaded the issue and gave the same reasons as in the previous letter. The colleagues' representatives refuted him on the spot, and Commissioner Guo had no words to reply after being refuted. He then threatened the colleagues with resignation, and the most important words were: "Guo is here only to support the difficult situation. If you force me too much, Guo will have to resign, and in the near future, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will close down." The colleagues believe that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is a state-owned institution, and Commissioner Guo is only a representative or a public servant of the institution. The colleagues' double salaries are requested from the institution based on the principle of equality and the purpose of improving or protecting the technology of the staff, and not from Commissioner's personal request. How can the personal request be exchanged for the personal interest of the staff ? The commissioner has been responsible for his task, which is beyond category. For the colleagues, the purpose is to ask for a better treatment, so in front of the commissioner, the commission will not take away the chance of the commissioner to back down for his lack of composure, but it has to be brought into public's attention so that the commission can ask for public criticism and aid. One-sidedly, it still hopes for the commission to reflect. In fact, based on the estimation, China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's capital will be nearly fifty million, and the lost is only over ten million. In addition, ship's business would less likely be on a loss, and the conclusion would be. If the fact that Commissioner Guo wants to shut down China Merchant Steam Navigation Company or not is completely another issue, every toddler would be able to realize it. Guo uses it as a means for coercing, coercing as a means for fighting to express how he treat his staff in oppression. Moreover, Commissioner Guo is not an expert of the shipping business. He is loyal, which makes him taken advantage of others. Today,Commissioner Guo seems like making people feel forced so that others have no backing down, so any losses in the Commission and those staff should be borne by Commissioner Guo.

Next, the staff salaries are to China Merchant Steam Navigation Company like a drop in the ocean, the Commission leaks up to at least ten times a month. Guo should exert his efforts to exert on others but not on the Commission. It is known Guo is being taken advantage by people. The Commission's goal today is salary equality. The Commission, as the position of today's staff, is reluctant to discuss since the commission only knows about one to two in the Bureau of Politics, silence would be better. As to asking for commission and facts, disclosure must be done so the public can decide.

Sincerely, The petition group of China Merchant Steam Navigation Company Crew One side, China merchants Steam Navigation company. July 1st Year twenty one

Zhang Qun Bids Farewell to the Citizens of Shanghai

Zhang Qun issued a farewell letter to the citizens of Shanghai, saying, "Time flies, and the seasons change. Since I was ordered to come to Shanghai in April of the 18th year of the Republic of China, it has been two years and nine months. I have lived with the people of Shanghai, and now I am fortunate to be relieved of my burden and return to my original post. I cannot help but express my feelings of parting and offer a few words of parting advice for your consideration. Looking back on my residence in Shanghai, I have spent a total of twenty years, and since the 1911 Revolution, I have followed the people of Shanghai and the martyrs in fighting together and dedicating my blood. Although I have occasionally traveled around for national affairs, I have been familiar with the people of Shanghai and have been frank and sincere in sharing hardships for a long time. Shanghai has become my second hometown. I have been honored with Shanghai's governance and have received the unreserved support and encouragement of the people, enabling me to devote my efforts to municipal administration and promote progress. Building a nine-仞 mountain cannot be accomplished in a day, and planting trees for ten years cannot be expected to bear fruit in the morning. Shanghai has many affairs to be addressed, and it is difficult to handle them all at once. Although I have dedicated my revolutionary enthusiasm and exhausted my wisdom and ability, I have always strived to realize the early construction of a great Shanghai, but I am ashamed of my lack of talent and the difficulties of the times. In addition, I have been repeatedly ordered to travel for national affairs, and I have not been able to settle down. As a result, my talent is short, my heart is long, my ambitions are great, and my achievements are small. My duties have been neglected, and my measures have been difficult to implement as expected. Looking back on the past and examining the present, my achievements that have greatly benefited the citizens are actually few. However, the people of Shanghai have been tolerant of my shortcomings and have not held me responsible for small mistakes. When I resigned this time, they rushed to retain me, and I am even more ashamed of their kindness. I am flattered and grateful. The reason why I resolutely resigned this time is not to seek fame or to avoid difficulties and think of retreat. It is because in the past two or three years, internal and external troubles have been frequent, and since the Shenyang Incident in September, the government and the people have been shocked, and the world is in debt. Patriots are becoming more and more determined, and those who endanger the country are secretly spreading chaos. Shanghai is far and wide, and a corner concerns the overall situation. If the security is disturbed, the impact will be great. Therefore, I have been neglecting sleep and food, planning day and night, enduring humiliation and bearing burdens, and seeking appropriate responses. My heart and strength have been exhausted, and my spirit has been greatly damaged. If I were to support myself forcibly, it would lead to public and private exhaustion. Moreover, now that the whole party is harmonious and the central government is unified, the government must be repaired and invigorated. How can my tired body bear the burden of a hill? It is also appropriate to resign. Fortunately, the successor is competent. Mr. Wu Tiecheng has been newly appointed to come to Shanghai. Mr. Wu has a deep foundation in the history of the party and the country and a great reputation. The people of Shanghai should all follow his example. With his long-standing talent in coordinating national affairs, his familiarity with political affairs, his daily cultivation of scholarship, and his spirit of tempering, he will be able to handle Shanghai's political affairs with ease, and his great plans will be seen in the future. His achievements will undoubtedly be doubled compared to those of my days in office. I hope that the people of Shanghai will use the same enthusiasm as they did in supporting me to support Mr. Tiecheng, so that the construction of a great Shanghai and the completion of the city center can be expected soon. The new municipal government building has already held a groundbreaking ceremony and can be completed by the end of this year. For the sake of prudence, the Construction Fund Custody Committee of the City Center District has been established. After this, there will be no fear of depletion of construction funds, and there will be no impact from changes in the political situation. All measures can be carried out in an orderly manner. This is what I, even though I have retired as a citizen, am still very eager and happy about. What is even more important is that Shanghai is the center of national culture and the hub of domestic and foreign transportation. Everyone knows the importance of it. Since the fall of Liaoning and Jilin, the people have been excited and have cherished the ambition to save the country and the determination to go to the disaster. I deeply see the danger of destroying the house to get the child and I am even more aware of the lesson of turning over the nest to save the eggs. Therefore, I have united with the authorities and people from all walks of life to discuss sincerely and have established a meeting every Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday to gather the strength and broad knowledge. So that loving the country will not be just empty talk, and defending against insults can be seen in the future. I am seeking a sound plan to avoid the covetousness of violence, and my painstaking efforts may be understood in the end. Now that Jinzhou has fallen and foreign troubles are getting deeper, if there are too many lawsuits, it will only expose weaknesses. I hope that the citizens will maintain their pure patriotism, cultivate their spirits, align their steps, adhere to durability, and never give up. Every word and every action must follow the rules and defend the border. This will prevent them from having a chance to take advantage of us and allow us to make up for our mistakes. If we occasionally indulge in emotions and slightly break the defense, the danger of being slaughtered like fish will be even greater. This is what our loved ones are sad about and what our enemies are happy about. The great disaster in the future does not require divination. I think that the patriotic and pure citizens of Shanghai will not bear to do this. The support of a wide mansion is not just a single tree, and the aspirations of the people can form a city. Although I have retired as a citizen, I am still willing to follow the people from all walks of life as a citizen and devote my efforts to the plan of repairing and saving the country. In the past, Shaokang revived in a journey, and Goujian avenged his shame and gathered for ten years. Those who have accomplished great things and accomplished great causes in ancient and modern times have never succeeded without relying on unity and hard work. I respectfully give these words to my citizens and hope that we will work together to revitalize Shanghai and save the country. Sincerely,

Zou Lu's Statement Regarding the Northeast Generals' Telegram

The Northeast generals jointly sent a telegram when Jinzhou was lost, stating that they were forced to withdraw troops due to the lack of supplies and ammunition from the central government, and that the Northeast incident was due to Zou Lu's betrayal of the country and leading wolves into the house. Zou has now issued the following statement of responsibility: There is a newspaper report of a telegram from the Northeast generals, saying that I betrayed the country and led wolves into the house, etc. The Northeast generals have not signed their names. It can also be called an anonymous exposé. If Zhang Xueliang loses the three northeastern provinces, he wants to lightly push the blame for betraying the country onto others with a telegram. Even a three-year-old child will not be deceived by him. The accumulated cases amount to hundreds, causing the pretext for the Japanese invasion. Zhang Xueliang and his son concluded many secret agreements with Japan, resulting in the Northeast's diplomacy, and even to the point that the Japanese invaded Liaoning and Jilin, and they did not resist, resulting in the loss of two provinces within a few hours. Ma Zhanshan fought alone, with hundreds of thousands of soldiers, but they did not send reinforcements, resulting in the loss of Heilongjiang Province. Regarding the defense of Jinzhou, the central government repeatedly ordered strict resistance, but they disobeyed the order and withdrew their troops. These facts are seen by everyone. Even if they want to falsely accuse someone of betraying the country or leading wolves into the house, can they succeed? The reason why I provoked this telegram is because two months ago, I telegraphed Zhang Xueliang, saying that as the commander of the Northeast Border Defense, he lost the Northeast land and should immediately commit suicide to apologize to the people. After the withdrawal of troops from Jinzhou, I telegraphed the central government to strictly punish Zhang Xueliang to maintain discipline. It should be known that my telegram to Zhang Xueliang was entirely to make Zhang Xueliang clear his responsibility and apologize to the people, to maintain the attitude of a man. The request to strictly punish Zhang Xueliang was entirely to maintain discipline and clarify right and wrong, and I have no personal grudge against Zhang Xueliang. People of the country can understand by looking at the facts before and after, so there is no need for me to defend myself.

Hanshi Aviation Conducted a Test Flight Yesterday

The Hanshi air route, which is being prepared by China Aviation Corporation, had its Hankou to Laohekou section test-flown yesterday morning at 9:40 AM by pilot An Shengli in the Xuzhou aircraft. The company's Vice Chairman, Ban De, also took the flight to inspect the route and liaise with local governments. The section has a total of three stations: Hankou, Xiangyang, and Laohekou, with a total route length of over 700 li. The Xiangyang and Laohekou stations both use military airfields of the Ministry of Military Affairs. Once the test flight is completed, radio equipment will be installed, and the opening date will be determined. As for the Laohekou to Xi'an section, it is reported that the company is considering the need for it and will decide on the speed of its implementation. In the future, the entire route will be over 1,700 li and can be reached in four hours. Yesterday's test flight also carried 15 pounds of free mail from Hankou to the two stations.

Hongzhang Factory Fined for Not Affixing Stamp Duty to Account Books

The Hongzhang Textile Dyeing Factory on Gordon Road was reported for not affixing stamp duty to its account books. The Special District Stamp Duty Office sent personnel, along with police officers and judicial police, carrying a search warrant to conduct a search. Forty-eight account books were found on the spot that had not been affixed with stamp duty. All were handed over to the police for transfer to the First Special District Court for public prosecution. The trial was held at 9:00 AM yesterday morning. According to the representative who appeared in court, most of the factory's account books had already been stamped, and this was due to a lack of understanding of the regulations that led to the omission. Judge Shen fined the factory 10 yuan per book, for a total fine of 480 yuan, as a warning.

Local News Two

Shanghai, a Den of Vice

Theft of Property Worth 2.22 Million

17,000 Chinese and Foreign Criminals

Shanghai is a major port in East Asia, where criminals can easily hide. Although the police patrol day and night, the number of crimes is still the highest in the country. Taking the Public Concession as an example, there were 33 major murder cases and no fewer than 25 kidnapping cases reported to the police last year. Small theft cases are even more difficult to count. In total, the value of property robbed and stolen throughout the year reached a staggering 2,225,000 yuan. The police arrested over 17,000 Chinese and foreign criminals throughout the year and investigated a total of 18,000 cases. If the entire city is included, the number would be even higher.

Qimei Road and Huangxing Road Completed

Qimei Road, which is a shortcut from the Disiwei Road Moon Naijia Garden northward to the city center, is now completed with a full asphalt surface and is extremely flat. It takes only seven minutes by car from Disiwei Road to the city center via this road. In addition, the cinder surface of Huangxing Road, which runs from Ningguo Road directly to Xiangyin Road, is also completed and open to traffic. It takes only five minutes to drive, making it a shortcut from Yangshupu to the city center. The completion of the above two roads has made transportation in the city center area even more convenient.

Water Fees Should Be Calculated Based on Net Rent

The Real Estate Association Notifies Its Members

The Shanghai Real Estate Association issued a notice to all its members yesterday regarding the method of paying water fees, stating: "Dear Sirs, We believe that the case of the British Shanghai Waterworks Company charging additional fees on top of water fees is legally unreasonable. We have repeatedly negotiated without success and have been threatened with water cuts. The Shanghai Public Concession Bureau has clarified this illegal behavior and has decided that all water fees should be calculated based on the net rent, meaning that the amount of water fee should be deducted from the net rent that includes the water fee, and the water fee should be calculated based on the resulting amount. This matter is of great interest to landlords. Please take note."

Dispute over the Assessment of Rental Values for Tax Collection

The Taxpayers' Association Sends a Letter to the Public Works Department

The Shanghai Renters Association sent a letter to the Public Works Department of the Public Concession yesterday, stating: "Dear Sir, According to a letter from the Jingmei Printing Company at No. 2 Xingapore Road, our company is located at No. 2 Xingapore Road. Previously, the Public Works Department excessively overestimated the rent and collected taxes. We sent a letter to your department to argue our case based on reason. Later, Westerners from your department came to our office several times and requested that we change the rent to 130 taels per month to avoid further trouble, etc. Because your department was willing to lower the estimated rent quickly, we also sent someone to contact the general manager of your department, and we agreed to calculate the rent at a maximum of 110 taels per month. We were allowed to do so, and someone was sent to collect the donation and issued a receipt based on the monthly rent of 110 taels. Unexpectedly, on the 15th of this month (December), we received a letter from your department with a donation ticket for a monthly rent of 140 taels, instructing us to pay the remaining amount, etc. We then returned the donation ticket, stating that if you did not agree to calculate the rent at 110 taels per month, you could return the silver ticket, and we could send a letter to your department, etc. On the 22nd, your department sent another form, instructing us to sign and fill it out. Our company is a commercial legal entity, and we are busy with business every day. We originally hoped that your department would handle all public security matters in the concession. Unexpectedly, your department handles donations like a child's play, changing its mind frequently and creating unnecessary troubles. Our company is unable to bear these disturbances. In addition to returning the form to your department, we are sending a special letter to your department, requesting that you inform your department that if you agree to calculate the monthly rent at 110 taels, you can come to collect it later. If you cannot agree, our company is willing to rent the house to your department at 150 taels per month. In addition, we will not reply to any further letters from your department, etc. We previously sent a letter to your department, requesting that you investigate and handle this matter. Now, the actions of the company are inconsistent, which is not conducive to the credibility of your government and is greatly hampered. With the approval of the letter, we respectfully request that you investigate and handle the matter as soon as possible in accordance with the agreement of 110 taels of rent per month. Yours sincerely, Shanghai Public Concession Public Works Department General Manager."

New Vegetable Market Opens on Beijing Road

The base is lower, preventing encroachment

The road base is raised to facilitate drainage

A new vegetable market, recently built by the Public Works Department, has opened east of Beijing Road and Fujian Road on January 2nd. Mr. Zhou Dengjun, Director of the Sanitation Department of the Bureau, observed that in the vegetable markets in various places, vendors arbitrarily moved their stalls, encroaching on the roads, causing extreme congestion for those buying vegetables. Also, because vegetable vendors sprinkled a lot of water, water accumulated everywhere in the market. Therefore, the newly built Beijing Road vegetable market was specially designed with the roads in the market built two or three inches higher than the stall bases on both sides, and the roads were built in an arch shape to facilitate drainage. In this way, the wooden stalls cannot encroach on the roads, and water will not accumulate in the market. This greatly improves the order of the vegetable market and the convenience of vegetable buyers. The vegetable market is currently two stories high and can accommodate more than two hundred stalls. Another floor can be added. The buildings are solid and the style is quite beautiful. The light and air are very sufficient. The front faces Beijing Road. Four shops are set up downstairs and have all been rented out. The staircase facing the street on the second floor of the vegetable market is also built here. The back of the vegetable market faces the Suzhou River. The downstairs is rented to a land goods shop, but the road surface has also been widened so that the loading and unloading of large quantities of vegetables will not obstruct traffic.

Bandits Hijack Car for Half a Day

The Motive Remains Unknown

Yesterday morning at 7:40 AM, a customer arrived at the Republic Automobile Company at 549 Avenue Edward VII. Claiming to be surnamed Gu, he rented a car to go to 4 Tatary, Scott Road. Chauffeur Hou Liansheng drove the Shanghai-registered car number 637, French Concession number 12595, taking the passenger who claimed to be surnamed Gu to the aforementioned location. Unexpectedly, upon arriving near 4 Tatary, four or five people were already waiting there. All of them were holding handguns. After the car stopped, they swarmed into the car, ordering the chauffeur not to make a sound. Then, the bandits drove the car straight towards Ningguo Road. At a deserted location, they let the chauffeur go after having him guarded by two bandits for a long time. The chauffeur then reported the incident to the 5th District, 4th Precinct Public Security Bureau and the Yangshupu Police Station, requesting an investigation. Around 1:30 PM, the car hijacked by the bandits was suddenly discovered in front of the Anhui Guild Hall on Zhongxing Road in Zhabei. A police sergeant reported this to the 4th District Public Security Bureau, who then took the car to the main bureau, awaiting the owner to claim it.

Li Yunpeng Commits Suicide

Left a Suicide Note Apologizing to the Hotel

Claimed to Spiritually Protect Their Business Development

At the Xiangxing Inn, number 6, 8 Mile Bridge Road, West Xinzha Road, around 4 PM the day before yesterday, a young man arrived. He was wearing a white-gray cotton robe, Western-style trousers, and leather shoes. The tea attendant led him to room number 11 on the third floor. He paid a deposit of six dimes for the room. He wrote down "Li Yunpeng from Ningbo, 22 years old, bookseller" in the register. Soon after, he started writing a letter in the room, appearing quite happy. Around 7 PM, he called the tea attendant for dinner. Afterward, he went out to mail the letter. Upon returning, he bought a newspaper. Nothing unusual happened that night. Yesterday morning at 8 AM, he got up and paced alone in the room, looking unwell. Between 9 and 10 AM, the tea attendant heard a sound of something hitting the wall coming from room number 11. He immediately went inside to check and saw the man’s face pale. He heard moaning sounds coming from his throat. He found a bottle of Atolin sleeping pills on the table, but the pills were all gone, and a suicide note. The tea attendant accompanied him to the Western Tibet Road Epidemic Hospital for treatment. The inn even paid a dollar for the registration fee. It was said that Li had taken too much poison and his life was in danger. The suicide note is attached below: To the esteemed management of the hotel: I am writing to inform you that I find life meaningless, so I have decided to commit suicide. Because I have no suitable place to die, I have reluctantly come to your hotel to use it temporarily as my final resting place. I, Yunpeng, cannot contribute to society and only eat the rice of the nation, so I think it is best to commit suicide. However, I feel very sorry for dying in your hotel. I can only ask the hotel owner to understand. If I have a spirit after death, I will definitely protect the development of your hotel business. Please acknowledge this. Respectfully, Li Yunpeng, January 6th.

A Story of an Unfortunate Romance with a Fan

Like a Fragment of an Old Novel

Now Resulting in a Lawsuit

Jiang Gongyu, the owner of Dafeng Lace Store at number 323, East Gonghe Lane, Fuzhou Road, was standing in front of his store enjoying the cool air on the evening of the third day of the fifth month of the lunar calendar. A female traveler named Qi Yuying, staying at the adjacent Jiangsu Inn, accidentally dropped her fan in front of Jiang. Jiang looked up and saw the young and beautiful woman. He couldn't help but be moved. He picked up the fan and took it upstairs to her room, using the opportunity to express his affection. He learned that the woman was from Caonitan, Jiashan, 19 years old, and still a young maiden. She had come to Shanghai with her cousin Wang Lanying to shop for her wedding dowry and was staying at the inn. Jiang took advantage of the fact that Qi's companions had gone out shopping and started to seduce her. Yuying was indeed charmed, and Jiang opened another room for them to have a good time together, vowing to stay together forever. After Qi returned to her hometown, Jiang could not forget her. On June 26th, he went to Jiashan to visit her and then brought her back to Shanghai to stay temporarily at the Central Hotel. Once his desire was satisfied, he allowed her to return home. Unexpectedly, on November 29th, he again brought her to Shanghai to live together at number 37, West Lin Road. Eventually, Jiang's wife found out, and a jealous dispute arose. They moved back to the Jiangsu Inn. Qi's mother, Qi Xi, after her beloved daughter disappeared, sent her son Qi Yunxiang to search for her everywhere. Recently, they found her. The mother said that her daughter had already been promised to a man surnamed Zhu, so how could she allow Jiang to have an affair with her? Moreover, Jiang was already a married man, so he should not defile a respectable girl. She hired a lawyer and filed a criminal lawsuit against Jiang at the First Special District Court, requesting that he be punished according to Article 257 of the criminal law for seducing a girl under 20 years old. She also filed a civil suit, requesting that the defendant be ordered to pay 5,000 yuan in compensation for damage to her reputation and 290 yuan for travel expenses. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Xiao of the First Special Court held a hearing. The defendant hired lawyer Qu Zheng to defend him. The lawyer argued that the preliminary issue in this case was to clarify jurisdiction before proceeding with the trial. After debating with the plaintiff's lawyer, Judge Ge confirmed that the defendant's residence was on West Lin Road, which was not under the jurisdiction of this court. The court announced that both parties should wait for the case to be transferred to the Shanghai District Court for trial.

Lawyers Should Not Insult Judges

Lawyer Liu Mingdu Sent to the Prosecutor's Office for Investigation

Lawyer Liu Du, representing Xu Xianglin in a cohabitation case with his wife Xu Shen, reached a settlement in the Civil Division of the District Court. Xu was to pay his wife living expenses every month. After the settlement, Xu Shen requested enforcement. Judge He Yuliu of the Execution Division of the court enforced the order according to the law, demanding payment from Xu Xianglin and ordering Xu's guarantor to report to the court. Failure to comply would result in detention. However, the lawyer did not understand that the judge was bound by the original case when enforcing the order. He filed a protest, arguing that Xu Shen had not fulfilled the conditions and that the judge should not act so forcefully. He accused the judge of being biased and violating the law. Judge He was greatly angered by this, believing that lawyers should not deliberately insult judges. The court treats all parties equally, and any accusation of illegal bias must be supported by evidence. Therefore, he reopened the execution hearing yesterday. The lawyer remained defiant, so the judge sent Lawyer Liu to the Prosecutor's Office for investigation.

Responsibility for a Bus Running Over a Worker

The Key Lies in Opening the Bus Door

Eyewitnesses Can Come Forward to Testify

At 6:15 PM on the 2nd of this month, Liu Guangxi, a worker at the Dafeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory, took bus number 15003 from Avenue Bai-li-nan to Gordon Road. Upon arriving at the stop, because there were many people waiting for the bus, the bus continued driving forward without stopping. Liu argued with the bus conductor, and Feng Bofang, a passenger who was an employee of the bus company, rang the bell to make the bus stop. Unexpectedly, as soon as Feng got off the bus, he stumbled and was run over by the bus. Indian constables arrived and took the injured person to Baolong Hospital for treatment, but he died. The police charged the ticket seller number 209 with negligence causing death and brought him to the First Special District Court for prosecution yesterday morning. Feng Bofang initially testified as a witness. After the police lawyer presented the case, ticket seller 209 testified that Feng was a coach in the bus company who specialized in training ticket sellers and should know all the regulations. Therefore, all ticket sellers should obey his orders. On that day, Feng saw that there were many passengers at the Gordon Road stop and ordered the bus not to stop. Later, when the deceased wanted to get off the bus, Feng opened the door and let him off, resulting in him being run over. However, at that time, I was selling tickets inside the bus, and I didn't open the door. Feng Bofang testified that he saw the deceased arguing with the ticket seller, and to avoid a dispute on the bus, he rang the bell to stop the bus and the ticket seller opened the door to let him off. Next, Mr. Danweier, representing the bus company, testified that Feng was not a coach or ticket seller. Bao Laigao, a friend of the deceased, testified that the deceased said in the hospital that the ticket seller opened the door halfway and pushed him off. Other witnesses testified that they saw the deceased being run over. Because the key to this case lies in opening the bus door and the testimonies of the witnesses and parties involved are contradictory, further investigation is needed. The court scheduled a retrial on the 12th of this month. Feng Bofang is temporarily detained. If anyone witnessed the whole truth on the bus that day, coming forward to testify would be beneficial to the case. It is hoped that they will come to court to testify at the next hearing.

Qihua Company's Special Treatment for Customers

Holding a Priceless Sale with a Big Raffle

The Qihua Company Limited on Nanjing Road is holding a priceless sale with a big raffle starting on the 7th. The so-called priceless sale means giving away goods without charging a price. From the 7th to the 31st, the company will lower prices for 25 days. After the 25-day period, they will invite celebrities to draw a date from the 25 dates in a fair and open manner. Customers can exchange their invoice for goods at the company based on the face value of the invoice from that day, without paying any extra money. In this way, goods are given away for free for one day out of the 25 days, hence the name priceless sale. The big raffle involves assigning a number to all invoices issued during the 25 days. After the 25 days are over, they will draw the raffle. The numbers drawn will correspond to the grand prize, second prize, third prize, and 30 small prizes. The grand prize winner will receive 400 yuan in company vouchers, the second prize winner 200 yuan, the third prize winner 100 yuan, and the small prize winners 10 yuan each. This business promotion with sacrifice greatly benefits customers.

Theft of More Than 30 Bicycles

Li Yousheng, detective of the Loujiawan French Police Station, and his deputy, Zeng Jiuru, along with detective Bao Jinrong, recently arrested habitual bicycle thieves Jiwei Monk, Wu Shichang, and Wang Renmao. They were brought to the police station and confessed to colluding in stealing more than 30 bicycles. They were sent to the Second Special District Court for detention pending investigation and verification. The police chief ordered the detectives to store the stolen bicycles at the police station, awaiting the owners to claim them.

Guanshengyuan Opens Another Branch

Guanshengyuan Food Company already has two branches in this city. In recent years, seeing that the market in the Xiaodongmen area of the South City is becoming increasingly prosperous and is approaching the level of the North City, in order to serve society and facilitate the public, they have specially organized a third branch there. They started operating last autumn, building a three-story Western-style building. The business area on the ground floor is modeled after the main store, and the second floor has been developed into a new-style tea room for people to rest and have refreshments. The interior and exterior decorations have been completed recently and it is scheduled to open tomorrow. It is said that candies and foods will be discounted for two weeks in commemoration.

Yitai Expands Business

Yitai Automobile Company, across from the Fairy World on Hubei Road, has been expanding its business recently. Because the original vehicles were insufficient to meet demand, they have made various efforts and acquired the Tengfei Automobile Company opposite the Shenzhou Hotel on Fuzhou Road the day before yesterday to expand their business as a branch of Yitai. It started operating yesterday.

The Shanghai Chinese Electrical Experiment Research Association was initiated by Zhuang Zhen, Li Jun, and other colleagues in the electrical industry. Its purpose is to promote electrical science and implement scientific salvation of the country. A permit will be issued, and the association should send a representative to the meeting to collect it. The document will be kept on file. It is said that the association has now received permit number 53 and is actively proceeding to show a unique color in the electrical industry.

Sincerely, Counselor of the Italian Embassy, Wan Dulin, January 7.
